* 9100: Aspects of the last things

* 9600: Hope

## 9010: Death (id: 9010)

* 9020: death
* 9030: dead bodies
* 9040: grave, the
* 9050: tombs
* **Associated Articles:** 9020: death (ID: `9020@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9030: dead bodies (ID: `9030@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9040: grave, the (ID: `9040@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9050: tombs (ID: `9050@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 9020: death (id: 9020)

Death in its various aspects is seen by Scripture as the opposite of God\-given life.

* **Associated Articles:** 9021: death, natural (ID: `9021@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9022: death, of believers (ID: `9022@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9023: death, of unbelievers (ID: `9023@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9024: death, spiritual (ID: `9024@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 9021: death, natural (id: 9021)

The end of life in the present world.

Death is natural to humanity as part of the created world
---------------------------------------------------------

**[ECC 12:7](https://ref.ly/Eccl12:7)** *See also* [PSA 39:5](https://ref.ly/Ps39:5), [PSA 104:29](https://ref.ly/Ps104:29); [ECC 3:18–3:21](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:18-Eccl3:21); [2PE 1:13–1:14](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:13-2Pet1:14)

Death is a result of Adam's sin
-------------------------------

**[ROM 5:12](https://ref.ly/Rom5:12)** *There is a tension between this text and those which suggest that death is a natural aspect of being human. Some suggest that the death referred to here is spiritual rather than physical.* *See also* [GEN 2:17](https://ref.ly/Gen2:17), [GEN 3:19](https://ref.ly/Gen3:19); [ROM 6:23](https://ref.ly/Rom6:23); [1CO 15:21–15:22](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:21-1Cor15:22)

Death is universal
------------------

### None can escape death

**[PSA 89:48](https://ref.ly/Ps89:48)** *See also* [GEN 6:3](https://ref.ly/Gen6:3); [JOS 23:14](https://ref.ly/Josh23:14); [2SA 14:14](https://ref.ly/2Sam14:14); [JOB 30:23](https://ref.ly/Job30:23)

### Death comes to all kinds of people

**[JOB 21:23–21:26](https://ref.ly/Job21:23-Job21:26)** *See also* [2SA 12:15–12:18](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:15-2Sam12:18); [2KI 4:20](https://ref.ly/2Kgs4:20); [PSA 37:35–37:36](https://ref.ly/Ps37:35-Ps37:36), [PSA 49:10](https://ref.ly/Ps49:10); [ECC 3:19](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:19); [LUK 16:22](https://ref.ly/Luke16:22)

### Only two people did not die

**[GEN 5:24](https://ref.ly/Gen5:24)**; **[2KI 2:11](https://ref.ly/2Kgs2:11)** *Enoch and Elijah died in the sense that their bodies were transformed from being suited to earthly life to life in heaven. They anticipated the death of Jesus Christ, whose body was not corrupted but transformed, and the transition to the new world of those who are alive when Jesus Christ comes again.*

Death is irreversible
---------------------

**[HEB 9:27](https://ref.ly/Heb9:27)** *The idea of reincarnation, that after death people repeatedly return to this life in a lower or higher form, is incompatible with death being once for all and an entrance into heaven or hell after the judgment.* *See also* [JOB 16:22](https://ref.ly/Job16:22); [PSA 115:17](https://ref.ly/Ps115:17)

Death is an aspect of human frailty
-----------------------------------

**[PSA 146:3–146:4](https://ref.ly/Ps146:3-Ps146:4)** *See also* [ISA 51:12](https://ref.ly/Isa51:12); [1PE 1:24](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:24); [ISA 40:6–40:8](https://ref.ly/Isa40:6-Isa40:8)

Death occurs when God determines it
-----------------------------------

**[JOB 14:5](https://ref.ly/Job14:5)** *See also* [DEU 32:39](https://ref.ly/Deut32:39); [JOB 38:17](https://ref.ly/Job38:17); [LUK 12:20](https://ref.ly/Luke12:20); [REV 1:18](https://ref.ly/Rev1:18)

The means of death
------------------

### Through old age

[GEN 25:8](https://ref.ly/Gen25:8), [GEN 35:29](https://ref.ly/Gen35:29); ; [JDG 8:32](https://ref.ly/Judg8:32); ; [1KI 2:10](https://ref.ly/1Kgs2:10)

### Through disease and accident

[2KI 1:2](https://ref.ly/2Kgs1:2), [2KI 1:16–1:17](https://ref.ly/2Kgs1:16-2Kgs1:17), [2KI 20:1](https://ref.ly/2Kgs20:1) parallel [2CH 32:24](https://ref.ly/2Chr32:24); ; [MRK 5:23](https://ref.ly/Mark5:23); ; [ACT 20:9](https://ref.ly/Acts20:9)

### Through violence

[JDG 9:5](https://ref.ly/Judg9:5), [JDG 9:52–9:54](https://ref.ly/Judg9:52-Judg9:54); ; [2SA 13:28–13:29](https://ref.ly/2Sam13:28-2Sam13:29); ; [1KI 15:28](https://ref.ly/1Kgs15:28); ; [2KI 8:14–8:15](https://ref.ly/2Kgs8:14-2Kgs8:15); ; [MAT 2:16](https://ref.ly/Matt2:16), [MAT 14:8–14:11](https://ref.ly/Matt14:8-Matt14:11)

### As a judgment by God

[LEV 10:1–10:2](https://ref.ly/Lev10:1-Lev10:2); ; [NUM 16:31–16:32](https://ref.ly/Num16:31-Num16:32), [NUM 20:23–20:24](https://ref.ly/Num20:23-Num20:24); ; [1SA 25:38](https://ref.ly/1Sam25:38); ; [2SA 6:7](https://ref.ly/2Sam6:7), [2SA 24:15](https://ref.ly/2Sam24:15); ; [2CH 13:20](https://ref.ly/2Chr13:20); ; [ACT 5:5](https://ref.ly/Acts5:5), [ACT 5:10](https://ref.ly/Acts5:10), [ACT 12:21–12:23](https://ref.ly/Acts12:21-Acts12:23); ; [1CO 11:29–11:30](https://ref.ly/1Cor11:29-1Cor11:30)

### Through a legal penalty

[EXO 21:12–21:17](https://ref.ly/Exod21:12-Exod21:17); ; [LUK 23:32](https://ref.ly/Luke23:32), [LUK 23:40–23:41](https://ref.ly/Luke23:40-Luke23:41)

The prospect of death affects human attitudes and values
--------------------------------------------------------

### Life is short

**[JAS 4:14](https://ref.ly/Jas4:14)** *See also* [JOB 7:6](https://ref.ly/Job7:6), [JOB 8:9](https://ref.ly/Job8:9), [JOB 9:25](https://ref.ly/Job9:25); [PSA 39:5](https://ref.ly/Ps39:5), [PSA 89:47](https://ref.ly/Ps89:47), [PSA 90:10](https://ref.ly/Ps90:10), [PSA 102:11](https://ref.ly/Ps102:11); [ECC 6:12](https://ref.ly/Eccl6:12); [ISA 38:12](https://ref.ly/Isa38:12), [ISA 40:6–40:8](https://ref.ly/Isa40:6-Isa40:8)

### People fear death

[PSA 18:4–18:6](https://ref.ly/Ps18:4-Ps18:6), [PSA 116:3](https://ref.ly/Ps116:3); ; [HEB 2:15](https://ref.ly/Heb2:15)

### People should prepare for death

**[2KI 20:1](https://ref.ly/2Kgs20:1)** parallel [ISA 38:1](https://ref.ly/Isa38:1) *See also* [PSA 39:4](https://ref.ly/Ps39:4), [PSA 90:12](https://ref.ly/Ps90:12); [AMO 4:12](https://ref.ly/Amos4:12)

### The expectation of death is an incentive to serve God

**[ECC 9:10](https://ref.ly/Eccl9:10)** *See also* [ISA 38:18–38:19](https://ref.ly/Isa38:18-Isa38:19); [JHN 9:4](https://ref.ly/John9:4)

### The expectation of death is an incentive to hold material blessings lightly

**[1TI 6:7](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:7)** *See also* [JOB 1:21](https://ref.ly/Job1:21); [LUK 12:13–12:21](https://ref.ly/Luke12:13-Luke12:21); [1CO 7:29–7:31](https://ref.ly/1Cor7:29-1Cor7:31)

Death is sometimes desired to escape problems
---------------------------------------------

[NUM 11:11–11:15](https://ref.ly/Num11:11-Num11:15); ; [1KI 19:4](https://ref.ly/1Kgs19:4); ; [JOB 3:11](https://ref.ly/Job3:11), [JOB 7:15](https://ref.ly/Job7:15); ; [JER 8:3](https://ref.ly/Jer8:3); ; [JON 4:3](https://ref.ly/Jonah4:3); ; [ACT 16:27](https://ref.ly/Acts16:27); ; [REV 9:6](https://ref.ly/Rev9:6)

Death was defeated by Jesus Christ
----------------------------------

**[2TI 1:10](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:10)** *See also* [ISA 25:8](https://ref.ly/Isa25:8); [HOS 13:14](https://ref.ly/Hos13:14); [1CO 15:24–15:26](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:24-1Cor15:26); [HEB 2:14](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14); [REV 20:14](https://ref.ly/Rev20:14)

There is no death in heaven
---------------------------

**[REV 21:4](https://ref.ly/Rev21:4)** *See also* [LUK 20:35–20:36](https://ref.ly/Luke20:35-Luke20:36); [2CO 5:1–5:2](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:1-2Cor5:2)

* **Associated Passages:** Ecclesiastes 12:7; Psalms 39:5; Psalms 104:29; Ecclesiastes 3:18-21; 2 Peter 1:13-14; Romans 5:12; Genesis 2:17; Genesis 3:19; Romans 6:23; 1 Corinthians 15:21-22; Psalms 89:48; Genesis 6:3; Joshua 23:14; 2 Samuel 14:14; Job 30:23; Job 21:23-26; 2 Samuel 12:15-18; 2 Kings 4:20; Psalms 37:35-36; Psalms 49:10; Ecclesiastes 3:19; Luke 16:22; Genesis 5:24; 2 Kings 2:11; Hebrews 9:27; Job 16:22; Psalms 115:17; Psalms 146:3-4; Isaiah 51:12; 1 Peter 1:24; Isaiah 40:6-8; Job 14:5; Deuteronomy 32:39; Job 38:17; Luke 12:20; Revelation 1:18; Genesis 25:8; Genesis 35:29; Judges 8:32; 1 Kings 2:10; 2 Kings 1:2; 2 Kings 1:16-17; 2 Kings 20:1; 2 Chronicles 32:24; Mark 5:23; Acts 20:9; Judges 9:5; Judges 9:52-54; 2 Samuel 13:28-29; 1 Kings 15:28; 2 Kings 8:14-15; Matthew 2:16; Matthew 14:8-11; Leviticus 10:1-2; Numbers 16:31-32; Numbers 20:23-24; 1 Samuel 25:38; 2 Samuel 6:7; 2 Samuel 24:15; 2 Chronicles 13:20; Acts 5:5; Acts 5:10; Acts 12:21-23; 1 Corinthians 11:29-30; Exodus 21:12-17; Luke 23:32; Luke 23:40-41; James 4:14; Job 7:6; Job 8:9; Job 9:25; Psalms 89:47; Psalms 90:10; Psalms 102:11; Ecclesiastes 6:12; Isaiah 38:12; Psalms 18:4-6; Psalms 116:3; Hebrews 2:15; Isaiah 38:1; Psalms 39:4; Psalms 90:12; Amos 4:12; Ecclesiastes 9:10; Isaiah 38:18-19; John 9:4; 1 Timothy 6:7; Job 1:21; Luke 12:13-21; 1 Corinthians 7:29-31; Numbers 11:11-15; 1 Kings 19:4; Job 3:11; Job 7:15; Jeremiah 8:3; Jonah 4:3; Acts 16:27; Revelation 9:6; 2 Timothy 1:10; Isaiah 25:8; Hosea 13:14; 1 Corinthians 15:24-26; Hebrews 2:14; Revelation 20:14; Revelation 21:4; Luke 20:35-36; 2 Corinthians 5:1-2
* **Associated Articles:** 2530: Jesus Christ, death of (ID: `2530@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 4015: life (ID: `4015@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5067: suicide (ID: `5067@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5281: crucifixion (ID: `5281@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5297: disease (ID: `5297@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5725: old age (ID: `5725@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5795: bereavement (ID: `5795@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6020: sin (ID: `6020@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6203: mortality (ID: `6203@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7346: death penalty (ID: `7346@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8357: weakness (ID: `8357@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9040: grave, the (ID: `9040@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 9022: death, of believers (id: 9022)

Believers in Jesus Christ will depart from this present life to the joy of God's presence.

Death is a normal experience for believers
------------------------------------------

**[ROM 14:8](https://ref.ly/Rom14:8)** *See also* [HEB 9:27](https://ref.ly/Heb9:27)

Death can be a blessing
-----------------------

### Because of the prospect of heaven

**[PHP 1:21–1:23](https://ref.ly/Phil1:21-Phil1:23)** *See also* [NUM 23:10](https://ref.ly/Num23:10); [PSA 49:15](https://ref.ly/Ps49:15), [PSA 116:15](https://ref.ly/Ps116:15); [LUK 2:29](https://ref.ly/Luke2:29); [2TI 4:6–4:8](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:6-2Tim4:8); [REV 7:13–7:17](https://ref.ly/Rev7:13-Rev7:17), [REV 14:13](https://ref.ly/Rev14:13)

### Because it brings relief from trouble and problems

[1KI 19:4](https://ref.ly/1Kgs19:4); ; [JOB 3:20](https://ref.ly/Job3:20), [JOB 7:15](https://ref.ly/Job7:15); ; [2TH 1:7](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:7)

At death believers are with Christ
----------------------------------

### They are in his presence

**[LUK 23:43](https://ref.ly/Luke23:43)** *See also* [2CO 5:8](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:8); [1TH 5:10](https://ref.ly/1Thess5:10)

### They are safe and secure

**[REV 2:11](https://ref.ly/Rev2:11)** *The second death is the final banishment of unbelievers from God's presence.* *See also* [ROM 14:8](https://ref.ly/Rom14:8); [REV 20:6](https://ref.ly/Rev20:6)

### They have the prospect of a new order of things

**[REV 21:4](https://ref.ly/Rev21:4)** *See also* [2TI 4:6–4:8](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:6-2Tim4:8); [REV 22:3–22:5](https://ref.ly/Rev22:3-Rev22:5)

The defeat of death
-------------------

### Death is vanquished for believers

**[1CO 15:55](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:55)** *See also* [ROM 8:36](https://ref.ly/Rom8:36); [2TI 1:10](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:10); [HEB 2:14](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14); [REV 20:14](https://ref.ly/Rev20:14)

### Death is to be reversed in resurrection

Though some of the above passages suggest that eternal life in Jesus Christ's presence is experienced immediately at death, others such as the following link these blessings with resurrection at the final coming of Jesus Christ: [JHN 11:23](https://ref.ly/John11:23); ; [1CO 15:51–15:54](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:51-1Cor15:54); ; [1TH 4:16](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:16)

The death of believers is likened to sleep
------------------------------------------

### Implying rest, renewing and awaking

**[ACT 7:59–7:60](https://ref.ly/Acts7:59-Acts7:60)** *Sleep does not imply lack of consciousness but rather rest, renewing and awaking. In the NT it is only used of believers.* *See also* [DEU 31:16](https://ref.ly/Deut31:16); [DAN 12:2](https://ref.ly/Dan12:2); [MRK 5:39](https://ref.ly/Mark5:39); [JHN 11:11–11:14](https://ref.ly/John11:11-John11:14); [ACT 13:36](https://ref.ly/Acts13:36); [1CO 15:6](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:6), [1CO 15:17–15:18](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:17-1Cor15:18); [1TH 4:13–4:16](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:13-1Thess4:16)

### Implying peace and comfort

**[LUK 16:22](https://ref.ly/Luke16:22)** *Abraham's side suggests a welcome to a place of peace and protection.* *See also* [GEN 49:33](https://ref.ly/Gen49:33); [2KI 22:20](https://ref.ly/2Kgs22:20); [ISA 57:1–57:2](https://ref.ly/Isa57:1-Isa57:2); [LUK 16:25](https://ref.ly/Luke16:25)

Death and the recognition of others
-----------------------------------

**[1TH 4:17](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:17)** *“caught up together” implies recognition.* *See also* [GEN 25:8](https://ref.ly/Gen25:8) *“gathered to his people” (literally “to his father's kin”) is a common OT expression and implies continued existence together*; [JOB 3:13–3:14](https://ref.ly/Job3:13-Job3:14); [MAT 17:4](https://ref.ly/Matt17:4); [MRK 9:4](https://ref.ly/Mark9:4); [LUK 16:24](https://ref.ly/Luke16:24); [1CO 13:12](https://ref.ly/1Cor13:12)

Believers can face death without fear
-------------------------------------

### They die in relationship with God

**[HEB 2:14–2:15](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14-Heb2:15)** *See also* [PSA 23:4](https://ref.ly/Ps23:4); [PRO 14:32](https://ref.ly/Prov14:32)

### They die trusting the Lord

[HEB 11:13](https://ref.ly/Heb11:13), [HEB 11:21–11:22](https://ref.ly/Heb11:21-Heb11:22)

### They receive comfort in facing death

**[JHN 11:25–11:26](https://ref.ly/John11:25-John11:26)** *See also* [ISA 25:8](https://ref.ly/Isa25:8); [1CO 15:26](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:26); [REV 1:18](https://ref.ly/Rev1:18)

### In death they can glorify God

**[PHP 1:20](https://ref.ly/Phil1:20)**

### In this believers are to be envied

**[NUM 23:10](https://ref.ly/Num23:10)**

Believers often hated the idea of death
---------------------------------------

*See also* [JOB 17:13–17:16](https://ref.ly/Job17:13-Job17:16); [PSA 9:13](https://ref.ly/Ps9:13); [ISA 38:10](https://ref.ly/Isa38:10); [ROM 8:36](https://ref.ly/Rom8:36); [1CO 15:55–15:56](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:55-1Cor15:56); [2CO 4:11–4:12](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:11-2Cor4:12)

Martyred believers are specially honoured in Scripture
------------------------------------------------------

**[REV 12:11](https://ref.ly/Rev12:11)** *See also* [REV 2:13](https://ref.ly/Rev2:13)

* **Associated Passages:** Romans 14:8; Hebrews 9:27; Philippians 1:21-23; Numbers 23:10; Psalms 49:15; Psalms 116:15; Luke 2:29; 2 Timothy 4:6-8; Revelation 7:13-17; Revelation 14:13; 1 Kings 19:4; Job 3:20; Job 7:15; 2 Thessalonians 1:7; Luke 23:43; 2 Corinthians 5:8; 1 Thessalonians 5:10; Revelation 2:11; Revelation 20:6; Revelation 21:4; Revelation 22:3-5; 1 Corinthians 15:55; Romans 8:36; 2 Timothy 1:10; Hebrews 2:14; Revelation 20:14; John 11:23; 1 Corinthians 15:51-54; 1 Thessalonians 4:16; Acts 7:59-60; Deuteronomy 31:16; Daniel 12:2; Mark 5:39; John 11:11-14; Acts 13:36; 1 Corinthians 15:6; 1 Corinthians 15:17-18; 1 Thessalonians 4:13-16; Luke 16:22; Genesis 49:33; 2 Kings 22:20; Isaiah 57:1-2; Luke 16:25; 1 Thessalonians 4:17; Genesis 25:8; Job 3:13-14; Matthew 17:4; Mark 9:4; Luke 16:24; 1 Corinthians 13:12; Hebrews 2:14-15; Psalms 23:4; Proverbs 14:32; Hebrews 11:13; Hebrews 11:21-22; John 11:25-26; Isaiah 25:8; 1 Corinthians 15:26; Revelation 1:18; Philippians 1:20; Job 17:13-16; Psalms 9:13; Isaiah 38:10; 1 Corinthians 15:55-56; 2 Corinthians 4:11-12; Revelation 12:11; Revelation 2:13
* **Associated Articles:** 2372: Jesus Christ, victory of (ID: `2372@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5059: rest, eternal (ID: `5059@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5535: sleep, and death (ID: `5535@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6644: eternal life (ID: `6644@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7903: baptism (ID: `7903@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8450: martyrdom (ID: `8450@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8481: self-sacrifice (ID: `8481@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8754: fear (ID: `8754@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9310: resurrection (ID: `9310@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9414: heaven, as community of the redeemed (ID: `9414@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9430: paradise (ID: `9430@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9610: hope (ID: `9610@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 9023: death, of unbelievers (id: 9023)

The departure from the present life of unrepentant people to await final banishment from God.

Death is inevitable
-------------------

**[PSA 49:10](https://ref.ly/Ps49:10), [PSA 89:48](https://ref.ly/Ps89:48)** *See also* [2SA 14:14](https://ref.ly/2Sam14:14); [JOB 30:23](https://ref.ly/Job30:23); [PSA 37:36](https://ref.ly/Ps37:36); [ECC 3:19–3:20](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:19-Eccl3:20), [ECC 8:8](https://ref.ly/Eccl8:8)

The premature death of unbelievers is the consequence of sin
------------------------------------------------------------

**[PRO 10:27](https://ref.ly/Prov10:27)** *OT writers, for whom God's blessing on the righteous occurs mostly in the present life, often saw early or sudden death as divine judgment on the wicked.* *See also* [1CH 10:13](https://ref.ly/1Chr10:13); [JOB 22:16](https://ref.ly/Job22:16); [PSA 9:17](https://ref.ly/Ps9:17), [PSA 37:1–37:2](https://ref.ly/Ps37:1-Ps37:2), [PSA 37:22](https://ref.ly/Ps37:22), [PSA 37:38](https://ref.ly/Ps37:38), [PSA 55:23](https://ref.ly/Ps55:23), [PSA 139:19](https://ref.ly/Ps139:19); [PRO 5:21–5:23](https://ref.ly/Prov5:21-Prov5:23), [PRO 11:19](https://ref.ly/Prov11:19), [PRO 14:12](https://ref.ly/Prov14:12); [ISA 17:14](https://ref.ly/Isa17:14); [EZK 3:19](https://ref.ly/Ezek3:19), [EZK 18:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:4), [EZK 18:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:20); [DAN 5:30](https://ref.ly/Dan5:30); [LUK 12:20](https://ref.ly/Luke12:20)

Aspects of the death of unbelievers
-----------------------------------

### They die unforgiven

[JHN 8:21](https://ref.ly/John8:21), [JHN 8:24](https://ref.ly/John8:24)

### They die without hope

[PRO 11:7](https://ref.ly/Prov11:7); ; [ECC 8:10](https://ref.ly/Eccl8:10)

### God has no pleasure in their death

**[EZK 18:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:23)** *See also* [EZK 18:32](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:32); [2PE 3:9](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:9)

Descriptions of the death of unbelievers
----------------------------------------

### Being destroyed

[MAT 7:13](https://ref.ly/Matt7:13); ; [ROM 9:22](https://ref.ly/Rom9:22)

### Perishing

[JHN 3:16](https://ref.ly/John3:16); ; [2PE 2:12](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:12)

### Being in fire

[LUK 16:22–16:24](https://ref.ly/Luke16:22-Luke16:24); ; [HEB 10:27](https://ref.ly/Heb10:27)

### Being in darkness

[MAT 25:30](https://ref.ly/Matt25:30); ; [2PE 2:17](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:17)

The consequences of the death of unbelievers
--------------------------------------------

### The intermediate state of awaiting judgment

**[REV 20:13](https://ref.ly/Rev20:13)** *See also* [LUK 16:23](https://ref.ly/Luke16:23); [JHN 5:29](https://ref.ly/John5:29); [ACT 24:15](https://ref.ly/Acts24:15)

### The judgment

**[HEB 9:27](https://ref.ly/Heb9:27)** *See also* [JHN 5:29](https://ref.ly/John5:29)

### The eternal consequences

**[DAN 12:2](https://ref.ly/Dan12:2)**; **[MAT 25:41](https://ref.ly/Matt25:41)** *See also* [MAT 18:8](https://ref.ly/Matt18:8), [MAT 25:46](https://ref.ly/Matt25:46); [MRK 9:45–9:48](https://ref.ly/Mark9:45-Mark9:48); [GAL 1:8–1:9](https://ref.ly/Gal1:8-Gal1:9); [HEB 6:2](https://ref.ly/Heb6:2); [JUD 1:7](https://ref.ly/Jude1:7)

## 9024: death, spiritual (id: 9024)

A condition in this life of alienation from God because of sin. It leads ultimately to the “second death”, the permanent separation of unbelievers from God.

Spiritual death means alienation from God in this life
------------------------------------------------------

**[EPH 2:1–2:3](https://ref.ly/Eph2:1-Eph2:3)**; **[COL 1:21](https://ref.ly/Col1:21)** *See also* [MAT 8:22](https://ref.ly/Matt8:22); [ROM 6:23](https://ref.ly/Rom6:23); [COL 2:13](https://ref.ly/Col2:13)

Spiritual death is a result of Adam's sin
-----------------------------------------

**[ROM 5:15–5:16](https://ref.ly/Rom5:15-Rom5:16)** *See also* [ROM 5:12](https://ref.ly/Rom5:12)

Symptoms of spiritual death
---------------------------

### Spiritual ignorance

[MAT 4:16](https://ref.ly/Matt4:16); ; [ISA 9:2](https://ref.ly/Isa9:2); ; [LUK 1:79](https://ref.ly/Luke1:79); ; [EPH 5:8](https://ref.ly/Eph5:8)

### A mind controlled by the sinful nature

**[ROM 8:5–8:8](https://ref.ly/Rom8:5-Rom8:8)** *See also* [PRO 8:36](https://ref.ly/Prov8:36), [PRO 14:12](https://ref.ly/Prov14:12), [PRO 16:25](https://ref.ly/Prov16:25), [PRO 21:16](https://ref.ly/Prov21:16); [EPH 4:18](https://ref.ly/Eph4:18)

### Unbelief

[JHN 3:36](https://ref.ly/John3:36); ; [1JN 5:12](https://ref.ly/1John5:12)

### Living in sinful pleasures

[LUK 15:13](https://ref.ly/Luke15:13); ; [1TI 5:6](https://ref.ly/1Tim5:6)

### Acting in ways that lead to death

[HEB 6:1](https://ref.ly/Heb6:1), [HEB 9:14](https://ref.ly/Heb9:14)

Spiritual death leads ultimately to the \`\`second death''
----------------------------------------------------------

[REV 2:11](https://ref.ly/Rev2:11), [REV 20:6](https://ref.ly/Rev20:6), [REV 20:14](https://ref.ly/Rev20:14), [REV 21:8](https://ref.ly/Rev21:8)

A church may be spiritually dead
--------------------------------

**[REV 3:1](https://ref.ly/Rev3:1)**

Deliverance from spiritual death is only through Jesus Christ
-------------------------------------------------------------

**[EPH 2:4–2:5](https://ref.ly/Eph2:4-Eph2:5)** *See also* [EZK 37:1–37:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:1-Ezek37:14); [LUK 15:24](https://ref.ly/Luke15:24), [LUK 15:32](https://ref.ly/Luke15:32); [JHN 5:24–5:25](https://ref.ly/John5:24-John5:25); [ROM 6:3–6:4](https://ref.ly/Rom6:3-Rom6:4), [ROM 6:13](https://ref.ly/Rom6:13)

## 9040: grave, the (id: 9040)

An OT synonym for death, the natural, inevitable human destiny, though not without hope for the righteous.

------------------------------

## 9050: tombs (id: 9050)

Graves or burial places, often cut out of rock. People were usually buried in family tombs and kings were often buried in royal tombs.

### Tombs cut out of rock

**[ISA 22:15–22:16](https://ref.ly/Isa22:15-Isa22:16)** *See also* [2KI 23:16](https://ref.ly/2Kgs23:16); [2CH 16:14](https://ref.ly/2Chr16:14); [MAT 27:59–27:60](https://ref.ly/Matt27:59-Matt27:60) parallels [MRK 15:46](https://ref.ly/Mark15:46), [LUK 23:53](https://ref.ly/Luke23:53)

-------------------

-------------------------

## 9105: last things (id: 9105)

The doctrine of the last things (“eschatology”) includes the subjects of death, the second coming of Jesus Christ, the resurrection of the dead, the last judgment, heaven and hell.

Death
-----

### Physical death is universal

**[JOB 30:23](https://ref.ly/Job30:23)** *See also* [2SA 14:14](https://ref.ly/2Sam14:14); [ROM 5:12](https://ref.ly/Rom5:12)

### The timing of natural death is beyond human control

**[ECC 8:8](https://ref.ly/Eccl8:8)** *See also* [PSA 90:10](https://ref.ly/Ps90:10); [MAT 6:27](https://ref.ly/Matt6:27); [JAS 4:14](https://ref.ly/Jas4:14)

### Death is not to be feared by the believer

**[PSA 23:4](https://ref.ly/Ps23:4)** *See also* [PSA 116:15](https://ref.ly/Ps116:15); [PRO 14:32](https://ref.ly/Prov14:32); [ROM 14:8](https://ref.ly/Rom14:8); [PHP 1:21](https://ref.ly/Phil1:21); [REV 14:13](https://ref.ly/Rev14:13)

### For believers, death is likened to falling asleep

**[JHN 11:11–11:13](https://ref.ly/John11:11-John11:13)** *See also* [MRK 5:39](https://ref.ly/Mark5:39); [ACT 13:36](https://ref.ly/Acts13:36); [1CO 15:6](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:6)

### At the second coming, believers still living on earth will not experience death

**[1TH 4:15–4:17](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:15-1Thess4:17)** *See also* [1CO 15:51–15:52](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:51-1Cor15:52)

### Death is the penalty for unforgiven sin

**[ROM 6:23](https://ref.ly/Rom6:23)** *See also* [1CH 10:13](https://ref.ly/1Chr10:13); [PRO 11:19](https://ref.ly/Prov11:19); [ROM 5:12](https://ref.ly/Rom5:12)

The second coming of Jesus Christ
---------------------------------

### The second coming is foretold

**[MAT 26:64](https://ref.ly/Matt26:64)** parallel [MRK 14:62](https://ref.ly/Mark14:62) *See also* [LUK 21:27](https://ref.ly/Luke21:27); [ACT 1:11](https://ref.ly/Acts1:11); [HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28)

### The timing of the second coming is known only to God the Father

**[MAT 24:36](https://ref.ly/Matt24:36)** parallel [MRK 13:32](https://ref.ly/Mark13:32) *See also* [MAL 3:1](https://ref.ly/Mal3:1); [MAT 24:44](https://ref.ly/Matt24:44) parallel [LUK 12:40](https://ref.ly/Luke12:40); [REV 16:15](https://ref.ly/Rev16:15)

### God's purpose at the second coming is to gather his people together, to reward the faithful and judge the wicked

**[MAT 16:27](https://ref.ly/Matt16:27)** *See also* [DAN 7:13–7:14](https://ref.ly/Dan7:13-Dan7:14); [MAT 25:31–25:32](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31-Matt25:32); [JHN 14:3](https://ref.ly/John14:3); [1CO 4:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor4:5); [1TH 4:16–4:17](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:16-1Thess4:17); [1PE 5:4](https://ref.ly/1Pet5:4); [1JN 3:2](https://ref.ly/1John3:2); [JUD 1:14–1:15](https://ref.ly/Jude1:14-Jude1:15)

### The right attitude towards the second coming

**[1JN 2:28](https://ref.ly/1John2:28)** *See also* [MRK 13:35](https://ref.ly/Mark13:35); [ACT 3:19–3:20](https://ref.ly/Acts3:19-Acts3:20); [1TI 6:13–6:14](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:13-1Tim6:14); [2PE 3:11](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:11)

The resurrection of the dead
----------------------------

### All will be raised

**[JHN 5:28–5:29](https://ref.ly/John5:28-John5:29)** *See also* [DAN 12:2](https://ref.ly/Dan12:2); [ACT 24:15](https://ref.ly/Acts24:15)

### Believers in Jesus Christ will be raised to eternal life

**[JHN 6:40](https://ref.ly/John6:40)** *See also* [JHN 11:25](https://ref.ly/John11:25); [2CO 4:14](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:14); [1TH 4:16](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:16)

### Unbelievers will be condemned

**[JHN 5:29](https://ref.ly/John5:29)** *See also* [MAT 25:46](https://ref.ly/Matt25:46)

### Believers will be given resurrection bodies

**[1CO 15:42–15:44](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:42-1Cor15:44)** *See also* [1CO 15:50–15:53](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:50-1Cor15:53)

The last judgment
-----------------

### All face judgment after death

**[HEB 9:27](https://ref.ly/Heb9:27)** *See also* [ROM 14:12](https://ref.ly/Rom14:12); [1PE 4:5](https://ref.ly/1Pet4:5); [REV 20:11–20:12](https://ref.ly/Rev20:11-Rev20:12)

### Judgment is entrusted to Jesus Christ

**[JHN 5:22](https://ref.ly/John5:22)** *See also* [ACT 10:42](https://ref.ly/Acts10:42), [ACT 17:31](https://ref.ly/Acts17:31); [REV 1:18](https://ref.ly/Rev1:18)

### Those who have not responded to Christ will be condemned

**[JHN 12:48](https://ref.ly/John12:48)** *See also* [2TH 1:7–1:8](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:7-2Thess1:8); [2PE 3:7](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:7); [JUD 1:15](https://ref.ly/Jude1:15); [REV 20:15](https://ref.ly/Rev20:15)

### Believers will not be judged for sin

**[JHN 5:24](https://ref.ly/John5:24)** *See also* [JHN 3:18](https://ref.ly/John3:18); [ROM 8:1–8:2](https://ref.ly/Rom8:1-Rom8:2), [ROM 8:33–8:34](https://ref.ly/Rom8:33-Rom8:34)

### Believers will be judged on how they have lived their Christian lives

**[2CO 5:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:10)** *See also* [1CO 4:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor4:5); [HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28); [1JN 4:17](https://ref.ly/1John4:17)

Heaven
------

### God's throne is in heaven where he is continuously worshipped

### God's will is perfectly served in heaven

**[REV 21:1](https://ref.ly/Rev21:1)**

### The redeemed will enjoy life in the presence of God in the new heaven

**[1TH 4:17](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:17)** *See also* [MAT 5:8](https://ref.ly/Matt5:8); [PHP 3:20](https://ref.ly/Phil3:20); [JUD 1:24](https://ref.ly/Jude1:24); [REV 21:1–21:4](https://ref.ly/Rev21:1-Rev21:4)

Hell
----

### Hell is the destiny of human beings who reject God

**[MAT 25:41](https://ref.ly/Matt25:41)** *Hell was originally meant for the punishment of the devil and his angels.* *See also* [MAT 13:41–13:42](https://ref.ly/Matt13:41-Matt13:42); [ROM 2:8](https://ref.ly/Rom2:8); [HEB 10:26–10:27](https://ref.ly/Heb10:26-Heb10:27); [JUD 1:6](https://ref.ly/Jude1:6); [REV 17:8](https://ref.ly/Rev17:8)

**[LUK 12:5](https://ref.ly/Luke12:5)** *See also* [MAT 5:29–5:30](https://ref.ly/Matt5:29-Matt5:30) *Jesus Christ is using Eastern hyperbole, not intended literally, to stress importance*; [MAT 13:40](https://ref.ly/Matt13:40)

## 9110: after-life (id: 9110)

Although the OT generally portrays this as a vague and shadowy existence, often associated with judgment, there are hints of the idea of resurrection to a fuller life which are developed in the NT. The NT points to judgment beyond death and to the believers' hope in resurrection, to a more complete enjoyment of God's presence and his blessings and to the promise of a new heaven and earth.

The after\-life in the OT
-------------------------

### The grave as a place of silence

**[PSA 115:17](https://ref.ly/Ps115:17)** *See also* [PSA 6:5](https://ref.ly/Ps6:5), [PSA 30:9](https://ref.ly/Ps30:9), [PSA 88:10–88:11](https://ref.ly/Ps88:10-Ps88:11); [ISA 38:18](https://ref.ly/Isa38:18)

### The grave as a place of darkness

**[JOB 10:21–10:22](https://ref.ly/Job10:21-Job10:22)** *See also* [1SA 2:9](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:9); [PSA 88:12](https://ref.ly/Ps88:12)

### The grave as a place of no return

**[JOB 7:8–7:10](https://ref.ly/Job7:8-Job7:10)** *See also* [JOB 16:22](https://ref.ly/Job16:22); [PSA 146:4](https://ref.ly/Ps146:4); [PRO 2:18–2:19](https://ref.ly/Prov2:18-Prov2:19); [ECC 12:7](https://ref.ly/Eccl12:7)

### The grave as a place of judgment

**[PSA 88:5](https://ref.ly/Ps88:5)** *See also* [PSA 31:17](https://ref.ly/Ps31:17); [PRO 9:18](https://ref.ly/Prov9:18); [ISA 14:9–14:11](https://ref.ly/Isa14:9-Isa14:11), [ISA 26:14](https://ref.ly/Isa26:14); [EZK 31:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek31:14), [EZK 32:17–32:32](https://ref.ly/Ezek32:17-Ezek32:32)

### The grave offers peace to the righteous

[JOB 3:13](https://ref.ly/Job3:13); ; [ECC 4:2](https://ref.ly/Eccl4:2); ; [ISA 57:1–57:2](https://ref.ly/Isa57:1-Isa57:2)

### The hope of resurrection

**[DAN 12:2](https://ref.ly/Dan12:2)** *See also* [JOB 19:26](https://ref.ly/Job19:26); [PSA 16:10–16:11](https://ref.ly/Ps16:10-Ps16:11), [PSA 49:15](https://ref.ly/Ps49:15), [PSA 73:24](https://ref.ly/Ps73:24); [ISA 25:7–25:8](https://ref.ly/Isa25:7-Isa25:8), [ISA 26:19](https://ref.ly/Isa26:19)

## 9115: antichrist, the (id: 9115)

One who is directly and implacably opposed to Jesus Christ.

--------------------------------------------------------------

**[2JN 1:7](https://ref.ly/2John1:7)** *See also* [MAT 24:24](https://ref.ly/Matt24:24) parallel [MRK 13:22](https://ref.ly/Mark13:22); [MRK 3:29](https://ref.ly/Mark3:29); [1JN 2:22](https://ref.ly/1John2:22), [1JN 4:3](https://ref.ly/1John4:3)

## 9120: eternity (id: 9120)

In Scripture eternity is not an abstraction but limitless time, over which God is totally sovereign.

* **Associated Articles:** 9121: eternity, nature of (ID: `9121@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9122: eternity, and God (ID: `9122@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 9121: eternity, nature of (id: 9121)

God alone possesses lasting time, in contrast to the fleeting time of the human race.

-------------------------------

**[PSA 90:4](https://ref.ly/Ps90:4)** *See also* [2PE 3:8](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:8)

--------------------------

## 9122: eternity, and God (id: 9122)

Whether one considers the past or the future, God alone is discovered to be permanent and lasting.

God's being, his wisdom and his word are eternal
------------------------------------------------

### God has always existed

**[GEN 1:1](https://ref.ly/Gen1:1)** *See also* [JOB 38:4](https://ref.ly/Job38:4); [PSA 90:2](https://ref.ly/Ps90:2); [HAB 1:12](https://ref.ly/Hab1:12); [JHN 1:1–1:2](https://ref.ly/John1:1-John1:2)

### The eternity of God's wisdom

**[PRO 8:22–8:23](https://ref.ly/Prov8:22-Prov8:23)** *See also* [HEB 9:14](https://ref.ly/Heb9:14); [1PE 1:20](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:20)

### God's word has always expressed his nature

**[PSA 119:89](https://ref.ly/Ps119:89)** *See also* [PSA 119:160](https://ref.ly/Ps119:160); [MAT 24:35](https://ref.ly/Matt24:35); [1PE 1:23–1:25](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:23-1Pet1:25); [ISA 40:8](https://ref.ly/Isa40:8)

God's purpose to bless is eternal
---------------------------------

## 9125: footstool (id: 9125)

Used mostly symbolically to refer to God's supreme authority over his creation. It is used especially to refer to his final victory over all those who oppose him.

The footstool as a rest for the feet
------------------------------------

**[2CH 9:18](https://ref.ly/2Chr9:18)**; **[JAS 2:3](https://ref.ly/Jas2:3)**

The footstool used symbolically
-------------------------------

### God's footstool as a symbol for the ark and the temple

**[PSA 132:7](https://ref.ly/Ps132:7)** *See also* [1CH 28:2](https://ref.ly/1Chr28:2); [PSA 99:5](https://ref.ly/Ps99:5); [LAM 2:1](https://ref.ly/Lam2:1)

### God's footstool as a symbol for the earth

**[ISA 66:1](https://ref.ly/Isa66:1)** *God cannot be confined to any man\-made temple.* *See also* [MAT 5:35](https://ref.ly/Matt5:35); [ACT 7:49](https://ref.ly/Acts7:49)

### Defeated enemies can be regarded as a footstool

[JOS 10:24–10:25](https://ref.ly/Josh10:24-Josh10:25); ; [1KI 5:3](https://ref.ly/1Kgs5:3); ; [PSA 66:12](https://ref.ly/Ps66:12); ; [ISA 51:23](https://ref.ly/Isa51:23); ; [MIC 7:10](https://ref.ly/Mic7:10)

### Jesus Christ will make all God's enemies his footstool

**[HEB 1:13](https://ref.ly/Heb1:13)** *This passage affirms Jesus Christ's supremacy over the angels.* *See also* [PSA 110:1](https://ref.ly/Ps110:1); [MAT 22:44](https://ref.ly/Matt22:44) parallels [MRK 12:36](https://ref.ly/Mark12:36), [LUK 20:43](https://ref.ly/Luke20:43); [ACT 2:34–2:35](https://ref.ly/Acts2:34-Acts2:35); [EPH 1:22](https://ref.ly/Eph1:22)

### Jesus Christ will complete his victory when he returns

**[HEB 10:13](https://ref.ly/Heb10:13)** *See also* [1CO 15:25](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:25); [HEB 2:8](https://ref.ly/Heb2:8); [PSA 8:6](https://ref.ly/Ps8:6)

* **Associated Passages:** 2 Chronicles 9:18; James 2:3; Psalms 132:7; 1 Chronicles 28:2; Psalms 99:5; Lamentations 2:1; Isaiah 66:1; Matthew 5:35; Acts 7:49; Joshua 10:24-25; 1 Kings 5:3; Psalms 66:12; Isaiah 51:23; Micah 7:10; Hebrews 1:13; Psalms 110:1; Matthew 22:44; Mark 12:36; Luke 20:43; Acts 2:34-35; Ephesians 1:22; Hebrews 10:13; 1 Corinthians 15:25; Hebrews 2:8; Psalms 8:6

## 9130: future, the (id: 9130)

God's promises about the future are certain because it is under God's control. Christians should live on the basis that these promises, which focus on the return of Jesus Christ, will be fulfilled.

God controls the future
-----------------------

### God knows the future

**[EXO 3:19–3:20](https://ref.ly/Exod3:19-Exod3:20)** *See also* [DEU 31:21](https://ref.ly/Deut31:21); [2SA 7:19](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:19) parallel [1CH 17:17](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:17); [PSA 139:4](https://ref.ly/Ps139:4); [ISA 42:9](https://ref.ly/Isa42:9), [ISA 46:10](https://ref.ly/Isa46:10); [DAN 2:28](https://ref.ly/Dan2:28); [ACT 2:23](https://ref.ly/Acts2:23), [ACT 3:18](https://ref.ly/Acts3:18)

### God can reveal the future

**[DAN 2:45](https://ref.ly/Dan2:45)** *See also* [GEN 15:13–15:16](https://ref.ly/Gen15:13-Gen15:16), [GEN 41:25](https://ref.ly/Gen41:25); [1SA 9:15–9:16](https://ref.ly/1Sam9:15-1Sam9:16); [2KI 8:10](https://ref.ly/2Kgs8:10); [DAN 8:19](https://ref.ly/Dan8:19), [DAN 10:14](https://ref.ly/Dan10:14); [MAT 2:13](https://ref.ly/Matt2:13); [ACT 18:9–18:10](https://ref.ly/Acts18:9-Acts18:10), [ACT 27:22–27:24](https://ref.ly/Acts27:22-Acts27:24)

The future is unknown to human beings
-------------------------------------

**[ECC 8:7](https://ref.ly/Eccl8:7)** *See also* [PRO 27:1](https://ref.ly/Prov27:1); [ECC 3:22](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:22), [ECC 7:14](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:14), [ECC 9:12](https://ref.ly/Eccl9:12), [ECC 10:14](https://ref.ly/Eccl10:14); [MAT 24:42–24:43](https://ref.ly/Matt24:42-Matt24:43); [ACT 20:22](https://ref.ly/Acts20:22); [JAS 4:14](https://ref.ly/Jas4:14)

------------------------------------

### It is based on God's promise

## 9135: immortality (id: 9135)

The quality of enduring into eternity, which Scripture insists belongs to God alone. However, God bestows the gift of eternal life and immortality upon those who believe and trust in him.

* **Associated Articles:** 9136: immortality, in OT (ID: `9136@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9137: immortality, in NT (ID: `9137@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 9136: immortality, in OT (id: 9136)

The OT stresses that God alone is immortal and indicates that this gift may be granted to human beings under certain conditions.

Immortality is an attribute of God
----------------------------------

### God is everlasting in himself

**[PSA 90:2](https://ref.ly/Ps90:2)** *See also* [NEH 9:5](https://ref.ly/Neh9:5); [PSA 41:13](https://ref.ly/Ps41:13); [ISA 9:6](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6), [ISA 40:28](https://ref.ly/Isa40:28); [HAB 1:12](https://ref.ly/Hab1:12)

### God is everlasting in his character and actions

**[DEU 33:27](https://ref.ly/Deut33:27)** *The way in which Scripture emphasises the character of God in these contexts shows that immortality is about a quality of being as well as about infinite duration.* [GEN 9:16](https://ref.ly/Gen9:16), [GEN 17:7](https://ref.ly/Gen17:7), [GEN 17:13](https://ref.ly/Gen17:13), [GEN 17:19](https://ref.ly/Gen17:19); ; [1CH 16:17](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:17) parallel [PSA 105:10](https://ref.ly/Ps105:10); [PSA 9:7](https://ref.ly/Ps9:7), [PSA 10:16](https://ref.ly/Ps10:16), [PSA 132:12](https://ref.ly/Ps132:12); ; [DAN 7:14](https://ref.ly/Dan7:14), [DAN 7:27](https://ref.ly/Dan7:27); [PSA 52:8](https://ref.ly/Ps52:8), [PSA 103:17](https://ref.ly/Ps103:17); ; [ISA 54:10](https://ref.ly/Isa54:10); ; [JER 31:3](https://ref.ly/Jer31:3); [PSA 119:142](https://ref.ly/Ps119:142); ; [DAN 9:24](https://ref.ly/Dan9:24); [ISA 45:17](https://ref.ly/Isa45:17) *God's everlasting salvation*; ; [ISA 54:8](https://ref.ly/Isa54:8) *God's everlasting kindness*; ; [ISA 60:19–60:20](https://ref.ly/Isa60:19-Isa60:20) *the LORD as the everlasting light*

Immortality is conditionally offered to human beings
----------------------------------------------------

**[GEN 3:22–3:23](https://ref.ly/Gen3:22-Gen3:23)** *See also* [PSA 6:5](https://ref.ly/Ps6:5), [PSA 88:5](https://ref.ly/Ps88:5), [PSA 88:10](https://ref.ly/Ps88:10), [PSA 115:17](https://ref.ly/Ps115:17); [DAN 12:2](https://ref.ly/Dan12:2) *The most specific OT reference to immortality. Note that while resurrection to judgment is for all, immortality is only for the righteous ([Pr 12:28](https://ref.ly/Prov12:28)).*

### Enoch and Elijah: two special cases

[GEN 5:24](https://ref.ly/Gen5:24); ; [2KI 2:11](https://ref.ly/2Kgs2:11)

The confidence of believers
---------------------------

**[PSA 16:9–16:11](https://ref.ly/Ps16:9-Ps16:11)** *See also* [PSA 17:15](https://ref.ly/Ps17:15), [PSA 21:6](https://ref.ly/Ps21:6), [PSA 73:24](https://ref.ly/Ps73:24), [PSA 133:3](https://ref.ly/Ps133:3)

### God will abolish death

**[ISA 25:8](https://ref.ly/Isa25:8)**

## 9137: immortality, in NT (id: 9137)

In the NT, immortal life is offered to human beings through Jesus Christ and guaranteed by the Holy Spirit. It is closely associated with eternal life and resurrection, but is seen more as a quality of being rather than in terms of unlimited extent.

Immortality is an attribute of God
----------------------------------

**[1TI 1:17](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:17)** *See also* [ROM 1:23](https://ref.ly/Rom1:23); [1TI 6:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:16)

-----------------------------------------------------------

**[2TI 1:10](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:10)** *See also* [JHN 6:50](https://ref.ly/John6:50), [JHN 8:51](https://ref.ly/John8:51), [JHN 11:26](https://ref.ly/John11:26); [1CO 15:22](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:22), [1CO 15:54](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:54)

Immortality is guaranteed by the Holy Spirit
--------------------------------------------

------------------------------------------------

## 9140: last days (id: 9140)

The final epoch of history which is marked by the coming of the Messiah and the establishment of God's kingdom. In the NT it is portrayed as the period between Jesus Christ's first coming and the consummation of all things at his return, and is marked by godlessness and the persecution of God's people.

OT expectation of the last days
-------------------------------

### The Messianic kingdom

**[ISA 2:2–2:4](https://ref.ly/Isa2:2-Isa2:4)** parallel [MIC 4:1–4:3](https://ref.ly/Mic4:1-Mic4:3) *See also* [ISA 9:6–9:7](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6-Isa9:7), [ISA 11:1–11:9](https://ref.ly/Isa11:1-Isa11:9), [ISA 65:20–65:25](https://ref.ly/Isa65:20-Isa65:25); [JER 33:15](https://ref.ly/Jer33:15)

### The restoration of Israel

**[JER 33:16](https://ref.ly/Jer33:16)**; **[HOS 3:5](https://ref.ly/Hos3:5)** *See also* [ISA 25:9](https://ref.ly/Isa25:9); [JER 30:9](https://ref.ly/Jer30:9), [JER 50:4](https://ref.ly/Jer50:4); [JOL 3:1](https://ref.ly/Joel3:1); [ZEC 8:23](https://ref.ly/Zech8:23)

### The day of the LORD

## 9145: Messianic age (id: 9145)

In the OT, writers look forward to the era that will be inaugurated by God's decisive intervention in human history, in order to establish his eternal kingdom under the Messiah. The Messianic age is characterised by righteousness, justice and peace, by the outpouring of the Holy Spirit and by the restoration and renewal of God's people and of creation. In the NT, the idea appears in a developed form as the “kingdom of God”, inaugurated by the first coming of Jesus Christ and to be consummated at his return.

The victory of God's kingdom foreseen
-------------------------------------

**[DAN 2:37–2:44](https://ref.ly/Dan2:37-Dan2:44)** *See also* [ZEC 14:9](https://ref.ly/Zech14:9)

### The victory of God's Messiah

**[PSA 45:3–45:6](https://ref.ly/Ps45:3-Ps45:6)** *This psalm came to be applied to the Messiah.* *See also* [PSA 110:5–110:6](https://ref.ly/Ps110:5-Ps110:6) *This psalm was also applied to the Messiah in the OT times*; [ISA 9:3–9:5](https://ref.ly/Isa9:3-Isa9:5), [ISA 42:13](https://ref.ly/Isa42:13), [ISA 59:17–59:19](https://ref.ly/Isa59:17-Isa59:19)

## 9150: Messianic banquet (id: 9150)

A symbolic portrayal of the blessings of the age to come in which those chosen by God share in a rich feast with the Messiah. In the NT this is often pictured as a marriage supper with Jesus Christ as the groom and the church as both bride and invited guests. The feast, which will take place after the consummation of God's kingdom, is prefigured in the Lord's Supper.

The Messianic banquet promised
------------------------------

**[ISA 25:6](https://ref.ly/Isa25:6)**; **[LUK 14:15](https://ref.ly/Luke14:15)**

The significance of banqueting
------------------------------

### As a sign of spiritual blessing

**[PSA 23:5](https://ref.ly/Ps23:5)** *See also* [JOB 36:16](https://ref.ly/Job36:16); [ISA 1:19](https://ref.ly/Isa1:19), [ISA 55:1–55:2](https://ref.ly/Isa55:1-Isa55:2); [JOL 2:24–2:26](https://ref.ly/Joel2:24-Joel2:26)

### As a sign of spiritual satisfaction

**[PSA 63:5](https://ref.ly/Ps63:5)** *See also* [PSA 107:9](https://ref.ly/Ps107:9); [ISA 58:11](https://ref.ly/Isa58:11); [EZK 34:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:14); [JHN 7:37–7:38](https://ref.ly/John7:37-John7:38); [REV 7:16–7:17](https://ref.ly/Rev7:16-Rev7:17)

### As a sign of fellowship with God

**[REV 3:20](https://ref.ly/Rev3:20)** *See also* [EXO 24:11](https://ref.ly/Exod24:11) *This may have been a covenant meal to seal the covenant between God and Israel*; [SNG 2:4](https://ref.ly/Song2:4)

The Messianic banquet as a wedding feast
----------------------------------------

### The invitation to participate

**[MAT 22:2](https://ref.ly/Matt22:2)**; **[REV 19:7–19:9](https://ref.ly/Rev19:7-Rev19:9)** *See also* [MAT 25:1–25:10](https://ref.ly/Matt25:1-Matt25:10); [LUK 14:16](https://ref.ly/Luke14:16); [REV 21:2](https://ref.ly/Rev21:2), [REV 21:9–21:10](https://ref.ly/Rev21:9-Rev21:10)

### The invitation rejected

[MAT 22:3–22:6](https://ref.ly/Matt22:3-Matt22:6); ; [LUK 14:16–14:20](https://ref.ly/Luke14:16-Luke14:20)

### The invitation given to others

**[MAT 8:11–8:12](https://ref.ly/Matt8:11-Matt8:12)** *See also* [MAT 22:7–22:14](https://ref.ly/Matt22:7-Matt22:14); [LUK 13:28–13:29](https://ref.ly/Luke13:28-Luke13:29), [LUK 14:21–14:24](https://ref.ly/Luke14:21-Luke14:24)

The anticipation of the Messianic banquet
-----------------------------------------

### Celebrating God's goodness

**[DEU 16:15](https://ref.ly/Deut16:15)** *See also* [NEH 8:10–8:12](https://ref.ly/Neh8:10-Neh8:12); [ZEC 14:16](https://ref.ly/Zech14:16)

### It is prefigured in the Lord's Supper

**[LUK 22:15–22:16](https://ref.ly/Luke22:15-Luke22:16)** *The Messianic banquet is here associated with the Passover meal which Jesus Christ shared with his disciples*; **[MAT 26:27–26:29](https://ref.ly/Matt26:27-Matt26:29)** parallels [MRK 14:23–14:25](https://ref.ly/Mark14:23-Mark14:25), [LUK 22:17–22:18](https://ref.ly/Luke22:17-Luke22:18)**[JHN 6:48–6:51](https://ref.ly/John6:48-John6:51)** *See also* [LUK 22:29–22:30](https://ref.ly/Luke22:29-Luke22:30); [JHN 6:55–6:56](https://ref.ly/John6:55-John6:56); [1CO 11:26](https://ref.ly/1Cor11:26)

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 25:6; Luke 14:15; Psalms 23:5; Job 36:16; Isaiah 1:19; Isaiah 55:1-2; Joel 2:24-26; Psalms 63:5; Psalms 107:9; Isaiah 58:11; Ezekiel 34:14; John 7:37-38; Revelation 7:16-17; Revelation 3:20; Exodus 24:11; Song of Songs 2:4; Matthew 22:2; Revelation 19:7-9; Matthew 25:1-10; Luke 14:16; Revelation 21:2; Revelation 21:9-10; Matthew 22:3-6; Luke 14:16-20; Matthew 8:11-12; Matthew 22:7-14; Luke 13:28-29; Luke 14:21-24; Deuteronomy 16:15; Nehemiah 8:10-12; Zechariah 14:16; Luke 22:15-16; Matthew 26:27-29; Mark 14:23-25; Luke 22:17-18; John 6:48-51; Luke 22:29-30; John 6:55-56; 1 Corinthians 11:26
* **Associated Articles:** 2230: Messiah, coming of (ID: `2230@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 4035: abundance (ID: `4035@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 4404: food (ID: `4404@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 4410: banquets (ID: `4410@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5710: marriage, customs concerning (ID: `5710@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6638: election (ID: `6638@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7020: church, the (ID: `7020@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7933: Lord's Supper (ID: `7933@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9145: Messianic age (ID: `9145@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 9155: millennium (id: 9155)

The period of 1,000 years referred to in Revelation chapter 20, during which Satan is bound and believers reign with Jesus Christ. This millennium is understood in different ways: as a period of unparalleled peace and prosperity for the church and the gospel at the end of this age, after which Christ will return (postmillennialism); as the time following Christ's return when he will reign on earth (premillennialism); as a symbolic reference to the period between Christ's first and second comings (amillennialism).

Characteristics of the millennium
---------------------------------

### Satan is bound

**[REV 20:1–20:3](https://ref.ly/Rev20:1-Rev20:3)** *“the Abyss” is the subterranean place of confinement for Satan and evil spirits.* *See also* [LUK 8:31](https://ref.ly/Luke8:31) parallels [MAT 8:29](https://ref.ly/Matt8:29), [MRK 5:7](https://ref.ly/Mark5:7)

### Martyred believers are raised to reign with Jesus Christ

**[REV 20:4–20:6](https://ref.ly/Rev20:4-Rev20:6)** *Those who have suffered for the gospel receive their promised reward.* *See also* [ROM 8:17](https://ref.ly/Rom8:17); [2TI 2:11–2:12](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:11-2Tim2:12); [REV 2:10](https://ref.ly/Rev2:10)

### Satan's release and final overthrow

**[REV 20:7–20:10](https://ref.ly/Rev20:7-Rev20:10)** *See also* [EZK 38:1–38:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek38:1-Ezek38:4), [EZK 38:15–38:16](https://ref.ly/Ezek38:15-Ezek38:16), [EZK 38:18–38:22](https://ref.ly/Ezek38:18-Ezek38:22), [EZK 39:2–39:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:2-Ezek39:5); [ZEC 14:2](https://ref.ly/Zech14:2); [ROM 16:20](https://ref.ly/Rom16:20)

The millennium will be a golden age on earth
--------------------------------------------

**[ISA 2:2–2:4](https://ref.ly/Isa2:2-Isa2:4)** parallel [MIC 4:1–4:3](https://ref.ly/Mic4:1-Mic4:3) *The OT looks forward to a period of universal peace and prosperity on earth. Both pre\- and postmillennialists see this as a reference to Jesus Christ's future earthly reign.* *See also* [ISA 11:6–11:9](https://ref.ly/Isa11:6-Isa11:9), [ISA 51:4–51:5](https://ref.ly/Isa51:4-Isa51:5), [ISA 65:25](https://ref.ly/Isa65:25)

The premillennial interpretation
--------------------------------

### The premillennial order of events

[REV 19:11–19:13](https://ref.ly/Rev19:11-Rev19:13) *Jesus Christ's return. Premillennialists understand the events of Revelation chapter 19 to precede those of Revelation chapter 20*; ; [REV 20:2–20:3](https://ref.ly/Rev20:2-Rev20:3) *Satan bound for 1,000 years*; ; [REV 20:4–20:6](https://ref.ly/Rev20:4-Rev20:6) *a “first resurrection” of believers to share Jesus Christ's reign over the earth*; ; [REV 20:7–20:10](https://ref.ly/Rev20:7-Rev20:10) *Satan's release and final overthrow*; ; [REV 20:11–20:15](https://ref.ly/Rev20:11-Rev20:15) *the general resurrection of all people to face God's judgment*

### A first resurrection of believers

**[1CO 15:22–15:25](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:22-1Cor15:25)** *This passage allows the idea of a gap between the resurrection of believers and the eternal age.* *See also* [1TH 4:16–4:17](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:16-1Thess4:17)

### God's future earthly reign

**[ZEC 14:9](https://ref.ly/Zech14:9)** *See also* [DAN 2:44](https://ref.ly/Dan2:44); [ZEP 3:11](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:11); [ZEC 14:16–14:21](https://ref.ly/Zech14:16-Zech14:21)

### Believers will reign with Jesus Christ

**[MAT 19:28](https://ref.ly/Matt19:28)** *Premillennialists take this to refer to an earthly reign.* *See also* [LUK 22:29–22:30](https://ref.ly/Luke22:29-Luke22:30); [1CO 6:2](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:2); [REV 5:9–5:10](https://ref.ly/Rev5:9-Rev5:10)

### Difficulties with premillennialism

Scriptures that depict a single resurrection of both the righteous and the wicked: [DAN 12:2](https://ref.ly/Dan12:2); ; [JHN 5:28–5:29](https://ref.ly/John5:28-John5:29); [MAT 13:40–13:43](https://ref.ly/Matt13:40-Matt13:43), [MAT 13:49–13:50](https://ref.ly/Matt13:49-Matt13:50), [MAT 25:31–25:32](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31-Matt25:32)

The postmillennial interpretation
---------------------------------

### The rapid spread of the gospel

**[MAT 24:14](https://ref.ly/Matt24:14)** parallel [MRK 13:10](https://ref.ly/Mark13:10) *See also* [MAT 13:31–13:33](https://ref.ly/Matt13:31-Matt13:33) parallels [MRK 4:31–4:32](https://ref.ly/Mark4:31-Mark4:32), [LUK 13:18–13:21](https://ref.ly/Luke13:18-Luke13:21)

### A future turning to God

[PSA 22:27–22:28](https://ref.ly/Ps22:27-Ps22:28); ; [ISA 19:19–19:24](https://ref.ly/Isa19:19-Isa19:24); ; [ZEC 2:11](https://ref.ly/Zech2:11)

### Difficulties with postmillennialism

The fortunes of the gospel and the church appear to be at a low ebb before Jesus Christ returns: [MAT 24:9–24:12](https://ref.ly/Matt24:9-Matt24:12) parallel [LUK 21:12–21:17](https://ref.ly/Luke21:12-Luke21:17); ; [2TI 3:1–3:5](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:1-2Tim3:5), [2TI 3:12–3:13](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:12-2Tim3:13); [MAT 28:18](https://ref.ly/Matt28:18); ; [ACT 2:33–2:36](https://ref.ly/Acts2:33-Acts2:36), [ACT 7:55–7:56](https://ref.ly/Acts7:55-Acts7:56)

The amillennial interpretation
------------------------------

### Satan was defeated at Jesus Christ's first coming

**[JHN 12:31](https://ref.ly/John12:31)** *See also* [MAT 12:29](https://ref.ly/Matt12:29) parallels [MRK 3:27](https://ref.ly/Mark3:27), [LUK 11:21–11:22](https://ref.ly/Luke11:21-Luke11:22); [LUK 10:18–10:20](https://ref.ly/Luke10:18-Luke10:20); [COL 2:14–2:15](https://ref.ly/Col2:14-Col2:15)

### Interpreting the \`\`first resurrection''

As a reference to the soul entering heaven after death: [LUK 23:43](https://ref.ly/Luke23:43); ; [2TI 4:7–4:8](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:7-2Tim4:8); [ROM 6:5](https://ref.ly/Rom6:5); ; [EPH 2:6](https://ref.ly/Eph2:6); ; [COL 3:1](https://ref.ly/Col3:1)

### Dangers of the amillennialist view

The future hope of believers is not only a spiritual reality: [ROM 8:19–8:21](https://ref.ly/Rom8:19-Rom8:21); ; [REV 21:1](https://ref.ly/Rev21:1); [1PE 5:8](https://ref.ly/1Pet5:8); ; [1JN 5:19](https://ref.ly/1John5:19); ; [REV 12:17](https://ref.ly/Rev12:17)

* **Associated Passages:** Revelation 20:1-3; Luke 8:31; Matthew 8:29; Mark 5:7; Revelation 20:4-6; Romans 8:17; 2 Timothy 2:11-12; Revelation 2:10; Revelation 20:7-10; Ezekiel 38:1-4; Ezekiel 38:15-16; Ezekiel 38:18-22; Ezekiel 39:2-5; Zechariah 14:2; Romans 16:20; Isaiah 2:2-4; Micah 4:1-3; Isaiah 11:6-9; Isaiah 51:4-5; Isaiah 65:25; Revelation 19:11-13; Revelation 20:2-3; Revelation 20:11-15; 1 Corinthians 15:22-25; 1 Thessalonians 4:16-17; Zechariah 14:9; Daniel 2:44; Zephaniah 3:11; Zechariah 14:16-21; Matthew 19:28; Luke 22:29-30; 1 Corinthians 6:2; Revelation 5:9-10; Daniel 12:2; John 5:28-29; Matthew 13:40-43; Matthew 13:49-50; Matthew 25:31-32; Matthew 24:14; Mark 13:10; Matthew 13:31-33; Mark 4:31-32; Luke 13:18-21; Psalms 22:27-28; Isaiah 19:19-24; Zechariah 2:11; Matthew 24:9-12; Luke 21:12-17; 2 Timothy 3:1-5; 2 Timothy 3:12-13; Matthew 28:18; Acts 2:33-36; Acts 7:55-56; John 12:31; Matthew 12:29; Mark 3:27; Luke 11:21-22; Luke 10:18-20; Colossians 2:14-15; Luke 23:43; 2 Timothy 4:7-8; Romans 6:5; Ephesians 2:6; Colossians 3:1; Romans 8:19-21; Revelation 21:1; 1 Peter 5:8; 1 John 5:19; Revelation 12:17

## 9160: new heavens and new earth (id: 9160)

A way of referring to the new creation that will come about at the end of time. The theme of the restoration and re\-creation of the world is a central aspect of the Christian hope.

The new heavens and new earth will replace the old
--------------------------------------------------

**[ISA 65:17](https://ref.ly/Isa65:17)** *See also* [HEB 12:26–12:27](https://ref.ly/Heb12:26-Heb12:27); [2PE 3:12–3:13](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:12-2Pet3:13); [REV 21:1](https://ref.ly/Rev21:1)

**[REV 21:3](https://ref.ly/Rev21:3)**

## 9165: restoration (id: 9165)

The returning of something or someone to their original state. Through the redeeming work of Jesus Christ, both humanity and creation will eventually be restored.

Restoration of human beings through the ministry of Jesus Christ
----------------------------------------------------------------

### Restoration of health

[LUK 4:38–4:39](https://ref.ly/Luke4:38-Luke4:39), [LUK 8:43–8:44](https://ref.ly/Luke8:43-Luke8:44), [LUK 14:2–14:4](https://ref.ly/Luke14:2-Luke14:4)

[MRK 7:32–7:35](https://ref.ly/Mark7:32-Mark7:35)

## 9170: signs of the times (id: 9170)

Portents marking significant historical events. In Scripture the phrase refers principally to signs indicating the coming of the Messiah and the kingdom of God (both in the ministry of Jesus Christ and at the end of time).

Signs of the times signifying the future deliverance of Judah
-------------------------------------------------------------

[2KI 19:29–19:31](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:29-2Kgs19:31) parallel [ISA 37:30–37:32](https://ref.ly/Isa37:30-Isa37:32) *The fruitfulness of the earth is to be a sign to Hezekiah that there will be a fruitful remnant of Judah.*

Signs of the times in the life of Jesus Christ
----------------------------------------------

### The virgin birth of Jesus Christ

**[ISA 7:14](https://ref.ly/Isa7:14)** *See also* [MAT 1:22–1:23](https://ref.ly/Matt1:22-Matt1:23)

### The miracles of Jesus Christ

**[MAT 12:28](https://ref.ly/Matt12:28)** parallel [LUK 11:20](https://ref.ly/Luke11:20) *See also* [JHN 2:11](https://ref.ly/John2:11), [JHN 2:23](https://ref.ly/John2:23), [JHN 3:2](https://ref.ly/John3:2), [JHN 4:54](https://ref.ly/John4:54), [JHN 6:2](https://ref.ly/John6:2), [JHN 6:14](https://ref.ly/John6:14), [JHN 9:16](https://ref.ly/John9:16), [JHN 11:47](https://ref.ly/John11:47), [JHN 12:17–12:18](https://ref.ly/John12:17-John12:18), [JHN 20:30](https://ref.ly/John20:30)

### Jesus Christ's resurrection

**[MAT 12:38–12:40](https://ref.ly/Matt12:38-Matt12:40)** parallel [LUK 11:29–11:30](https://ref.ly/Luke11:29-Luke11:30) *See also* [MAT 16:4](https://ref.ly/Matt16:4); [JHN 2:18–2:22](https://ref.ly/John2:18-John2:22)

### The Jews failed to perceive the signs of the times accompanying Jesus Christ's coming

**[MAT 16:1–16:4](https://ref.ly/Matt16:1-Matt16:4)** parallel [MRK 8:11–8:13](https://ref.ly/Mark8:11-Mark8:13) *See also* [LUK 12:54–12:56](https://ref.ly/Luke12:54-Luke12:56); [JHN 12:37](https://ref.ly/John12:37)

Signs of the times at the end of the age
----------------------------------------

**[MAT 24:3–24:14](https://ref.ly/Matt24:3-Matt24:14)** parallels [MRK 13:3–13:13](https://ref.ly/Mark13:3-Mark13:13), [LUK 21:7–21:19](https://ref.ly/Luke21:7-Luke21:19)**[LUK 21:25–21:28](https://ref.ly/Luke21:25-Luke21:28)** parallels [MAT 24:29–24:30](https://ref.ly/Matt24:29-Matt24:30), [MRK 13:24–13:26](https://ref.ly/Mark13:24-Mark13:26)

### It is impossible to predict the date of Jesus Christ's return from the signs of the times

**[1TH 5:1–5:2](https://ref.ly/1Thess5:1-1Thess5:2)**

Signs of the times signifying judgment
--------------------------------------

*See also* [ISA 20:3–20:4](https://ref.ly/Isa20:3-Isa20:4); [MAT 24:15–24:25](https://ref.ly/Matt24:15-Matt24:25) parallels [MRK 13:14–13:23](https://ref.ly/Mark13:14-Mark13:23), [LUK 21:20–21:24](https://ref.ly/Luke21:20-Luke21:24) *The fall of Jerusalem is itself a sign of the judgment of all people at the end of time.*

## 9210: judgment, God's (id: 9210)

God judges the world by identifying and condemning sin and by vindicating and rewarding the righteous. God exercises temporal judgment on the world and on his people; final judgment will take place when Jesus Christ returns.

The nature of God's judgment
----------------------------

### Its certainty

**[ECC 12:14](https://ref.ly/Eccl12:14)** *See also* [PSA 7:11](https://ref.ly/Ps7:11); [ECC 3:17](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:17), [ECC 11:9](https://ref.ly/Eccl11:9); [JAS 5:9](https://ref.ly/Jas5:9)

### Its righteousness

**[GEN 18:25](https://ref.ly/Gen18:25)** *See also* [PSA 9:7–9:8](https://ref.ly/Ps9:7-Ps9:8), [PSA 50:6](https://ref.ly/Ps50:6), [PSA 96:13](https://ref.ly/Ps96:13) parallel [1CH 16:33](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:33)

### Its impartiality

**[2CH 19:7](https://ref.ly/2Chr19:7)** *See also* [DEU 10:17](https://ref.ly/Deut10:17); [JOB 34:19](https://ref.ly/Job34:19); [PSA 98:9](https://ref.ly/Ps98:9); [ROM 2:11](https://ref.ly/Rom2:11); [EPH 6:9](https://ref.ly/Eph6:9)

The purpose of God's judgment
-----------------------------

### To display his glory

**[ISA 5:16](https://ref.ly/Isa5:16)** *See also* [EXO 14:4](https://ref.ly/Exod14:4); [ISA 59:18–59:19](https://ref.ly/Isa59:18-Isa59:19); [EZK 7:27](https://ref.ly/Ezek7:27), [EZK 38:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek38:23); [REV 14:7](https://ref.ly/Rev14:7)

### To vindicate the righteous

## 9220: day of the LORD (id: 9220)

The occasion of God's final intervention in human affairs to punish sin, restore the faithful of his people and establish his rule over the nations. It is linked with the Messianic hope and will be fulfilled at Jesus Christ's return. This future consummation is anticipated in historical acts of judgment and, although its time is unknown, it will be heralded and accompanied by signs and by great upheavals in nature.

The day of the LORD as a day of judgment
----------------------------------------

### Of universal judgment

**[ISA 24:21–24:22](https://ref.ly/Isa24:21-Isa24:22)** *See also* [ZEP 1:14–1:18](https://ref.ly/Zeph1:14-Zeph1:18)

### Of judgment on the nations

**[ISA 13:9–13:11](https://ref.ly/Isa13:9-Isa13:11)**; **[JER 46:10](https://ref.ly/Jer46:10)** *See also* [JOB 20:28–20:29](https://ref.ly/Job20:28-Job20:29); [ISA 13:4–13:6](https://ref.ly/Isa13:4-Isa13:6) *God's judgment on Babylon*[ISA 19:16–19:17](https://ref.ly/Isa19:16-Isa19:17); [EZK 30:3–30:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek30:3-Ezek30:4)[ISA 27:1](https://ref.ly/Isa27:1); [JOL 3:12–3:14](https://ref.ly/Joel3:12-Joel3:14); [OBA 1:15](https://ref.ly/Obad1:15) *God's judgment on Edom*; [ZEP 3:8](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:8); [ROM 2:16](https://ref.ly/Rom2:16); [REV 6:15–6:17](https://ref.ly/Rev6:15-Rev6:17)

## 9230: judgment seat (id: 9230)

The platform or throne from which kings and officials administer justice. God presently exercises judgment from his heavenly throne, symbolised in the OT by the ark of the covenant, and will one day bring all peoples before his judgment seat to give account of their lives and to receive their due reward.

Examples of earthly seats of judgment
-------------------------------------

## 9240: last judgment (id: 9240)

God's judgment of all people at the end of the age. This has been entrusted to Jesus Christ who, at his return, will reward the righteous and punish the unrighteous. Judgment will be on the basis of deeds, the response to God's revelation and faith in Jesus Christ. Believers need not fear the last judgment, but should live godly lives in anticipation of it.

The certainty of last judgment
------------------------------

**[HEB 9:27](https://ref.ly/Heb9:27)** *See also* [ECC 3:17](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:17); [ROM 14:10–14:12](https://ref.ly/Rom14:10-Rom14:12); [2CO 5:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:10); [1PE 4:5](https://ref.ly/1Pet4:5)

The time of last judgment
-------------------------

### It was anticipated in the cross

**[JHN 12:31](https://ref.ly/John12:31)** *Jesus Christ is speaking about his approaching death.*

### It will take place at the end of the age

**[MAT 13:49](https://ref.ly/Matt13:49)** *See also* [MAT 13:39–13:43](https://ref.ly/Matt13:39-Matt13:43)

### It will take place at Jesus Christ's return

**[2TH 1:6–1:7](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:6-2Thess1:7)** *See also* [MAT 25:31–25:33](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31-Matt25:33); [1CO 4:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor4:5); [2PE 3:10](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:10); [REV 19:11](https://ref.ly/Rev19:11)

Last judgment is the prerogative of God
---------------------------------------

### God as judge

**[DAN 7:9–7:10](https://ref.ly/Dan7:9-Dan7:10)** *See also* [HEB 12:23](https://ref.ly/Heb12:23)

### God entrusts judgment to Jesus Christ

**[ACT 17:31](https://ref.ly/Acts17:31)** *See also* [JHN 5:22](https://ref.ly/John5:22); [ACT 10:42](https://ref.ly/Acts10:42); [ROM 2:16](https://ref.ly/Rom2:16)

The result of last judgment
---------------------------

### Two eternal destinies

**[DAN 12:2](https://ref.ly/Dan12:2)** *See also* [MAT 25:46](https://ref.ly/Matt25:46)

### The ungodly will be punished

**[2PE 3:7](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:7)** *See also* [MAT 25:41](https://ref.ly/Matt25:41); [ROM 2:5](https://ref.ly/Rom2:5); [HEB 10:26–10:28](https://ref.ly/Heb10:26-Heb10:28); [2PE 2:4](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:4), [2PE 2:9](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:9); [JUD 1:6–1:7](https://ref.ly/Jude1:6-Jude1:7), [JUD 1:15](https://ref.ly/Jude1:15)

### The righteous will be rewarded

**[2TI 4:8](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:8)** *See also* [MAT 25:34](https://ref.ly/Matt25:34); [1CO 9:25](https://ref.ly/1Cor9:25); [REV 11:18](https://ref.ly/Rev11:18)

The basis of God's last judgment
--------------------------------

### It is according to works

**[REV 20:11–20:15](https://ref.ly/Rev20:11-Rev20:15)** *See also* [MAT 12:36–12:37](https://ref.ly/Matt12:36-Matt12:37), [MAT 16:27](https://ref.ly/Matt16:27); [ROM 2:6–2:10](https://ref.ly/Rom2:6-Rom2:10); [REV 22:12](https://ref.ly/Rev22:12)

### It is according to revelation

**[ROM 2:12](https://ref.ly/Rom2:12)** *See also* [MAT 11:20–11:24](https://ref.ly/Matt11:20-Matt11:24) parallel [LUK 10:13–10:15](https://ref.ly/Luke10:13-Luke10:15) *Those towns and cities which have rejected the revelation that Christ brings will face final judgment and condemnation*; [MAT 12:41–12:42](https://ref.ly/Matt12:41-Matt12:42) parallel [LUK 11:31–11:32](https://ref.ly/Luke11:31-Luke11:32)ROM [1:18–1:21](https://ref.ly/Luke1:18-Luke1:21), [ROM 2:14–2:15](https://ref.ly/Rom2:14-Rom2:15), [ROM 3:23](https://ref.ly/Rom3:23); [GAL 3:1](https://ref.ly/Gal3:1)

### It is according to attitude to Jesus Christ

**[JHN 3:18](https://ref.ly/John3:18)** *The only basis for salvation is faith in Jesus Christ.* *See also* [MAT 10:14–10:15](https://ref.ly/Matt10:14-Matt10:15) parallel [LUK 10:11–10:12](https://ref.ly/Luke10:11-Luke10:12) *Those towns which reject Jesus Christ's messengers will face judgment*; [MAT 10:32–10:33](https://ref.ly/Matt10:32-Matt10:33) parallel [LUK 12:8–12:9](https://ref.ly/Luke12:8-Luke12:9) *Those who disown Jesus Christ will be disowned by him*; [MAT 25:35–25:40](https://ref.ly/Matt25:35-Matt25:40); [MRK 8:38](https://ref.ly/Mark8:38); [LUK 10:16](https://ref.ly/Luke10:16); [ACT 4:12](https://ref.ly/Acts4:12), [ACT 16:30–16:31](https://ref.ly/Acts16:30-Acts16:31)

-----------------------------------

## 9250: woe (id: 9250)

An exclamation of judgment upon God's enemies, or of misfortune on oneself, or, in the ministry of Jesus Christ, of sadness over those who fail to recognise the true misery of their condition.

Woe as an exclamation of judgment on others
-------------------------------------------

### Woe to God's enemies

**[ISA 33:1](https://ref.ly/Isa33:1)** *Probably referring to Assyria.* *See also* [JER 48:1–48:2](https://ref.ly/Jer48:1-Jer48:2); [NAM 3:1–3:7](https://ref.ly/Nah3:1-Nah3:7); [HAB 2:6–2:20](https://ref.ly/Hab2:6-Hab2:20); [ZEP 2:5](https://ref.ly/Zeph2:5)

### Woe to God's faithless people

**[HOS 7:13–7:16](https://ref.ly/Hos7:13-Hos7:16)** *See also* [ISA 30:1–30:2](https://ref.ly/Isa30:1-Isa30:2), [ISA 45:9–45:10](https://ref.ly/Isa45:9-Isa45:10); [JER 4:13–4:18](https://ref.ly/Jer4:13-Jer4:18); [EZK 16:23–16:27](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:23-Ezek16:27)

### Woe to careless leaders of God's people

**[JER 23:1–23:2](https://ref.ly/Jer23:1-Jer23:2)** *See also* [EZK 13:1–13:9](https://ref.ly/Ezek13:1-Ezek13:9), [EZK 34:1–34:10](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:1-Ezek34:10); [ZEP 3:1–3:4](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:1-Zeph3:4); [ZEC 11:15–11:17](https://ref.ly/Zech11:15-Zech11:17)

**[AMO 6:1–6:7](https://ref.ly/Amos6:1-Amos6:7)** *See also* [AMO 5:18–5:24](https://ref.ly/Amos5:18-Amos5:24)

### Woe to those who neglect social justice

**[ISA 10:1–10:4](https://ref.ly/Isa10:1-Isa10:4)** *See also* [ISA 5:8–5:23](https://ref.ly/Isa5:8-Isa5:23); [JER 22:13–22:19](https://ref.ly/Jer22:13-Jer22:19); [MIC 2:1–2:3](https://ref.ly/Mic2:1-Mic2:3)

### Woe to a godless world

**[REV 8:13](https://ref.ly/Rev8:13)** *See also* [REV 12:12](https://ref.ly/Rev12:12), [REV 18:10](https://ref.ly/Rev18:10), [REV 18:16–18:17](https://ref.ly/Rev18:16-Rev18:17), [REV 18:19](https://ref.ly/Rev18:19)

## 9300: Resurrection (id: 9300)

* 9310: resurrection
* **Associated Articles:** 9310: resurrection (ID: `9310@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 9310: resurrection (id: 9310)

The raising of Jesus Christ from the dead by God after his suffering and death on the cross. Historical evidence for his resurrection includes the empty tomb and the appearance of the risen Christ to the disciples. It has significance both in relation to the identity of Jesus Christ and the future hope of believers.

* **Associated Articles:** 9311: resurrection, of Jesus Christ (ID: `9311@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9312: resurrection, significance of Jesus Christ's (ID: `9312@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9313: resurrection, spiritual (ID: `9313@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9314: resurrection, of the dead (ID: `9314@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9315: resurrection, of believers (ID: `9315@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 9311: resurrection, of Jesus Christ (id: 9311)

The resurrection of Jesus Christ is of central importance to the NT. It affirms the divinity of Jesus Christ, marks the words and deeds of his ministry with God's seal of approval and opens the way to the future resurrection of believers.

Jesus Christ's resurrection was foreshadowed in the OT
------------------------------------------------------

In Abraham and Isaac: [GEN 22:5](https://ref.ly/Gen22:5); ; [HEB 11:19](https://ref.ly/Heb11:19); [JON 1:17](https://ref.ly/Jonah1:17), [JON 2:10](https://ref.ly/Jonah2:10); ; [MAT 12:40](https://ref.ly/Matt12:40)

Jesus Christ's resurrection was predicted
-----------------------------------------

### In the OT

**[1CO 15:3–15:4](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:3-1Cor15:4)** *See also* [ISA 53:11](https://ref.ly/Isa53:11); [HOS 6:2](https://ref.ly/Hos6:2); [LUK 24:45–24:46](https://ref.ly/Luke24:45-Luke24:46); [ACT 2:25–2:31](https://ref.ly/Acts2:25-Acts2:31), [ACT 13:35](https://ref.ly/Acts13:35); [PSA 16:8–16:11](https://ref.ly/Ps16:8-Ps16:11); [ACT 13:34](https://ref.ly/Acts13:34), [ACT 26:22–26:23](https://ref.ly/Acts26:22-Acts26:23)

### By Jesus Christ himself

**[MAT 16:21](https://ref.ly/Matt16:21)** parallels [MRK 8:31](https://ref.ly/Mark8:31), [LUK 9:22](https://ref.ly/Luke9:22) *See also* [MAT 17:9](https://ref.ly/Matt17:9) parallel [MRK 9:9](https://ref.ly/Mark9:9); [MAT 20:18–20:19](https://ref.ly/Matt20:18-Matt20:19) parallels [MRK 10:32–10:34](https://ref.ly/Mark10:32-Mark10:34), [LUK 18:31–18:33](https://ref.ly/Luke18:31-Luke18:33); [MAT 26:32](https://ref.ly/Matt26:32) parallel [MRK 14:28](https://ref.ly/Mark14:28); [JHN 2:19–2:21](https://ref.ly/John2:19-John2:21)

Jesus Christ's resurrection was anticipated by the raising of the dead
----------------------------------------------------------------------

### In the OT

**[HEB 11:35](https://ref.ly/Heb11:35)** *None of the OT or NT miracles are true resurrections. Those raised resumed life as before, their bodies unchanged. Resurrection for Jesus Christ and therefore for his people means a changed body and permanent life in glory. This is the “better resurrection”.* *See also* [1KI 17:22](https://ref.ly/1Kgs17:22); [2KI 4:35](https://ref.ly/2Kgs4:35), [2KI 13:21](https://ref.ly/2Kgs13:21)

### In the miracles of Jesus Christ

**[LUK 7:22](https://ref.ly/Luke7:22)** parallel [MAT 11:4–11:5](https://ref.ly/Matt11:4-Matt11:5) *See also* [MAT 9:23–9:25](https://ref.ly/Matt9:23-Matt9:25) parallel [MRK 5:38–5:42](https://ref.ly/Mark5:38-Mark5:42); [MAT 27:52–27:53](https://ref.ly/Matt27:52-Matt27:53); [LUK 7:14–7:15](https://ref.ly/Luke7:14-Luke7:15); [JHN 11:43–11:44](https://ref.ly/John11:43-John11:44)

The sequence of events in Jesus Christ's resurrection
-----------------------------------------------------

### It was preceded by suffering and death

**[PHP 2:8–2:9](https://ref.ly/Phil2:8-Phil2:9)** *See also* [JHN 19:28–19:33](https://ref.ly/John19:28-John19:33); [HEB 2:9](https://ref.ly/Heb2:9)

### It took place on the first day of the week

[JHN 20:1–20:2](https://ref.ly/John20:1-John20:2) parallels [MAT 28:1–28:2](https://ref.ly/Matt28:1-Matt28:2), [MRK 16:2–16:4](https://ref.ly/Mark16:2-Mark16:4), [LUK 24:1–24:3](https://ref.ly/Luke24:1-Luke24:3)

### It was announced by angels

**[MAT 28:5–28:6](https://ref.ly/Matt28:5-Matt28:6)** parallels [MRK 16:5–16:6](https://ref.ly/Mark16:5-Mark16:6), [LUK 24:4–24:6](https://ref.ly/Luke24:4-Luke24:6) *See also* [LUK 24:23](https://ref.ly/Luke24:23); [1TI 3:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim3:16)

### The disciples were reluctant to believe it

## 9312: resurrection, significance of Jesus Christ's (id: 9312)

Jesus Christ's resurrection represents a demonstration of the power of God, the confirmation of the divinity of Jesus Christ and the grounds of hope for Christian believers.

Jesus Christ's resurrection was a demonstration of God's power
--------------------------------------------------------------

### The power of God the Father

**[EPH 1:18–1:20](https://ref.ly/Eph1:18-Eph1:20)** *See also* [MAT 22:29–22:32](https://ref.ly/Matt22:29-Matt22:32); [ACT 2:24](https://ref.ly/Acts2:24), [ACT 3:15](https://ref.ly/Acts3:15), [ACT 10:40](https://ref.ly/Acts10:40), [ACT 13:29–13:30](https://ref.ly/Acts13:29-Acts13:30); [GAL 1:1](https://ref.ly/Gal1:1); [COL 2:12](https://ref.ly/Col2:12)

### The power of the Holy Spirit

[ROM 1:4](https://ref.ly/Rom1:4); ; [1TI 3:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim3:16); ; [1PE 3:18](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:18)

The resurrection confirmed Jesus Christ as the Son of God
---------------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 20:30–20:31](https://ref.ly/John20:30-John20:31)** *John calls Jesus Christ's miracles “signs” (see also [Jn 2:11](https://ref.ly/John2:11); [6:2](https://ref.ly/John6:2)) and his resurrection is the climax, confirming his identity beyond all doubt*; **[ROM 1:4](https://ref.ly/Rom1:4)** *See also* [PSA 2:7](https://ref.ly/Ps2:7); [ACT 13:33](https://ref.ly/Acts13:33)

The centrality of the resurrection of Jesus Christ
--------------------------------------------------

### As the basis of faith

**[1CO 15:14–15:15](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:14-1Cor15:15)** *See also* [ACT 3:15](https://ref.ly/Acts3:15), [ACT 4:33](https://ref.ly/Acts4:33), [ACT 17:18](https://ref.ly/Acts17:18), [ACT 24:21](https://ref.ly/Acts24:21); [ROM 10:9](https://ref.ly/Rom10:9); [2TI 2:8](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:8); [HEB 6:1–6:2](https://ref.ly/Heb6:1-Heb6:2)

### As the basis of believers' justification

[ROM 4:25](https://ref.ly/Rom4:25), [ROM 8:34](https://ref.ly/Rom8:34)

### As the basis of Christian hope

[ACT 24:15](https://ref.ly/Acts24:15); ; [1CO 15:19](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:19)

### As the basis of believers' resurrection

**[1CO 15:20–15:23](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:20-1Cor15:23)** *The Law of Moses ([Ex 23:16](https://ref.ly/Exod23:16)) provided for an offering of the firstfruits of crops to God. The firstfruits were the guarantee of the full harvest to come. The NT sees the resurrection of Jesus Christ as the firstfruits of the full ingathering of all God's people when Jesus Christ comes again.* *See also* [JHN 14:19](https://ref.ly/John14:19); [ACT 26:23](https://ref.ly/Acts26:23); [ROM 8:11](https://ref.ly/Rom8:11)

* **Associated Passages:** Ephesians 1:18-20; Matthew 22:29-32; Acts 2:24; Acts 3:15; Acts 10:40; Acts 13:29-30; Galatians 1:1; Colossians 2:12; Romans 1:4; 1 Timothy 3:16; 1 Peter 3:18; John 20:30-31; John 2:11; John 6:2; Psalms 2:7; Acts 13:33; 1 Corinthians 15:14-15; Acts 4:33; Acts 17:18; Acts 24:21; Romans 10:9; 2 Timothy 2:8; Hebrews 6:1-2; Romans 4:25; Romans 8:34; Acts 24:15; 1 Corinthians 15:19; 1 Corinthians 15:20-23; Exodus 23:16; John 14:19; Acts 26:23; Romans 8:11
* **Associated Articles:** 1105: God, power of (ID: `1105@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2066: Jesus Christ, power of (ID: `2066@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2218: Jesus Christ, Son of God (ID: `2218@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2420: gospel (ID: `2420@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 3030: Holy Spirit, power of (ID: `3030@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8020: faith (ID: `8020@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9610: hope (ID: `9610@DictionaryBibleThemes`)

## 9315: resurrection, of believers (id: 9315)

The future event of finally being raised to glory with Jesus Christ. Believers may rest assured that, on account of their faith, they will share in the resurrection and glory of Christ and be with him for ever.

## 9410: heaven (id: 9410)

God's habitation where he is worshipped and served by angels. Solely on account of the sacrifice of Jesus Christ on the cross, believers will inherit a place in heaven and there for ever enjoy perfect fellowship with God in his worship and service.

* **Associated Articles:** 9411: heaven, nature of (ID: `9411@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9412: heaven, worship and service in (ID: `9412@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9413: heaven, inheritance of (ID: `9413@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9414: heaven, as community of the redeemed (ID: `9414@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 9411: heaven, nature of (id: 9411)

Scripture refers to heaven as God's habitation but also uses the term as an alternative for God himself.

Heaven as God's habitation
--------------------------

### It is the place where he dwells

**[DEU 26:15](https://ref.ly/Deut26:15)** *See also* [GEN 28:17](https://ref.ly/Gen28:17); [2CH 6:21](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:21); [ECC 5:2](https://ref.ly/Eccl5:2); [REV 13:6](https://ref.ly/Rev13:6)

### It is insufficient as God's dwelling\-place

**[1KI 8:27](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:27)** parallel [2CH 6:18](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:18) *See also* [PSA 113:5–113:6](https://ref.ly/Ps113:5-Ps113:6)

-----------------------------------

Heaven as an alternative term for God
-------------------------------------

**[LUK 15:18](https://ref.ly/Luke15:18)** *See also* [MAT 8:11](https://ref.ly/Matt8:11), [MAT 13:11](https://ref.ly/Matt13:11) *Matthew is writing especially for Jews who, out of reverence, tried to avoid using the word “God”. [Mk 4:11](https://ref.ly/Mark4:11) and [Lk 8:10](https://ref.ly/Luke8:10) prefer “kingdom of God”*; [MAT 16:19](https://ref.ly/Matt16:19), [MAT 18:18](https://ref.ly/Matt18:18), [MAT 21:25](https://ref.ly/Matt21:25) parallels [MRK 11:30](https://ref.ly/Mark11:30), [LUK 20:4](https://ref.ly/Luke20:4); [JHN 3:27](https://ref.ly/John3:27), [JHN 17:1](https://ref.ly/John17:1)

Heaven and the sovereignty of God
---------------------------------

### Heaven is the place of God's rule

**[DAN 4:26](https://ref.ly/Dan4:26)** *See also* [PSA 45:6](https://ref.ly/Ps45:6), [PSA 103:19](https://ref.ly/Ps103:19); [ACT 17:24](https://ref.ly/Acts17:24)

### God's voice from heaven speaks with divine authority

**[DEU 4:36](https://ref.ly/Deut4:36)** *See also* [DAN 4:31](https://ref.ly/Dan4:31); [JHN 12:28](https://ref.ly/John12:28); [1TH 4:16](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:16); [2PE 1:17–1:18](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:17-2Pet1:18)

Heaven glimpsed by human eyes
-----------------------------

### At the baptism of Jesus Christ

**[MRK 1:10](https://ref.ly/Mark1:10)** parallels [MAT 3:16](https://ref.ly/Matt3:16), [LUK 3:21–3:22](https://ref.ly/Luke3:21-Luke3:22) *See also* [JHN 1:32](https://ref.ly/John1:32)

### In visions

**[ACT 7:56](https://ref.ly/Acts7:56)** *See also* [2CO 12:2–12:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor12:2-2Cor12:4); [REV 4:1](https://ref.ly/Rev4:1)

Prayer addressed to God in heaven
---------------------------------

**[1KI 8:30](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:30)** *See also* [DEU 26:15](https://ref.ly/Deut26:15); [2CH 30:27](https://ref.ly/2Chr30:27); [NEH 1:4](https://ref.ly/Neh1:4); [PSA 20:6](https://ref.ly/Ps20:6); [REV 5:8](https://ref.ly/Rev5:8)

------------------------------------

**[MAT 23:22](https://ref.ly/Matt23:22)** *See also* [GEN 24:3](https://ref.ly/Gen24:3); [DAN 12:7](https://ref.ly/Dan12:7); [MAT 5:34](https://ref.ly/Matt5:34); [JAS 5:12](https://ref.ly/Jas5:12)

-----------------------------------

### His pre\-existence in heaven
