## 9412: heaven, worship and service in (id: 9412)

All in heaven engage continuously in the worship of God, while they perfectly carry out his will.

All heaven worships God
-----------------------

### The multitude in heaven and the twenty\-four elders

**[REV 19:6–19:7](https://ref.ly/Rev19:6-Rev19:7)** *See also* [NEH 9:6](https://ref.ly/Neh9:6); [REV 4:6–4:11](https://ref.ly/Rev4:6-Rev4:11), [REV 7:11–7:12](https://ref.ly/Rev7:11-Rev7:12), [REV 11:16](https://ref.ly/Rev11:16), [REV 22:8–22:9](https://ref.ly/Rev22:8-Rev22:9)

### The redeemed

**[1PE 2:9](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:9)** *See also* [ISA 51:11](https://ref.ly/Isa51:11); [REV 19:5–19:7](https://ref.ly/Rev19:5-Rev19:7)

### The angels

[LUK 2:13–2:14](https://ref.ly/Luke2:13-Luke2:14); ; [REV 5:11–5:12](https://ref.ly/Rev5:11-Rev5:12), [REV 7:11](https://ref.ly/Rev7:11)

### God is worshipped in song

**[REV 15:2–15:3](https://ref.ly/Rev15:2-Rev15:3)** *See also* [REV 14:3](https://ref.ly/Rev14:3)

### Jesus Christ is worshipped in heaven

**[PHP 2:10–2:11](https://ref.ly/Phil2:10-Phil2:11)** *See also* [DAN 7:14](https://ref.ly/Dan7:14); [HEB 1:6](https://ref.ly/Heb1:6); [REV 5:8–5:14](https://ref.ly/Rev5:8-Rev5:14)

All heaven serves God
---------------------

### God's will is perfectly done in heaven

**[MAT 6:10](https://ref.ly/Matt6:10)** *See also* [MAT 12:50](https://ref.ly/Matt12:50)

### The redeemed will serve God

**[REV 22:3](https://ref.ly/Rev22:3)** *See also* [REV 5:10](https://ref.ly/Rev5:10), [REV 7:13–7:15](https://ref.ly/Rev7:13-Rev7:15)

### The redeemed will reign with Jesus Christ and share his authority

[MAT 19:28](https://ref.ly/Matt19:28), [MAT 25:34](https://ref.ly/Matt25:34); ; [1CO 6:3](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:3); ; [2TI 2:12](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:12); ; [HEB 12:28](https://ref.ly/Heb12:28); ; [REV 2:26–2:27](https://ref.ly/Rev2:26-Rev2:27), [REV 3:21](https://ref.ly/Rev3:21), [REV 20:6](https://ref.ly/Rev20:6)

## 9413: heaven, inheritance of (id: 9413)

Heaven is the secure inheritance, of priceless value, awaiting the redeemed. There, faithful service will be rewarded and the redeemed will be given resurrection bodies for service in the heavenly realm.

Believers inherit the kingdom of heaven
---------------------------------------

### Their inheritance is secure

**[MAT 25:34](https://ref.ly/Matt25:34)** *See also* [LUK 12:32](https://ref.ly/Luke12:32), [LUK 22:28–22:29](https://ref.ly/Luke22:28-Luke22:29); [JAS 2:5](https://ref.ly/Jas2:5)

### The value of their inheritance is beyond human calculation

**[1CO 2:9–2:10](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:9-1Cor2:10)** *See also* [ACT 20:32](https://ref.ly/Acts20:32); [EPH 1:18](https://ref.ly/Eph1:18), [EPH 2:6–2:7](https://ref.ly/Eph2:6-Eph2:7)

### As those adopted into God's family they are heirs of God and Christ

**[ROM 8:17](https://ref.ly/Rom8:17)** *See also* [GAL 4:7](https://ref.ly/Gal4:7); [TIT 3:7](https://ref.ly/Titus3:7); [HEB 6:17](https://ref.ly/Heb6:17)

The nature of the heavenly inheritance
--------------------------------------

### It is inviolable

**[1PE 1:3–1:5](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:3-1Pet1:5)** *See also* [REV 21:25](https://ref.ly/Rev21:25), [REV 21:27](https://ref.ly/Rev21:27)

### It is a response to faith and love

**[JAS 2:5](https://ref.ly/Jas2:5)** *See also* [COL 1:12](https://ref.ly/Col1:12), [COL 3:24](https://ref.ly/Col3:24); [HEB 11:7](https://ref.ly/Heb11:7)

### It is for overcomers

**[REV 21:7](https://ref.ly/Rev21:7)** *See also* [1JN 4:4](https://ref.ly/1John4:4), [1JN 5:3–5:5](https://ref.ly/1John5:3-1John5:5); [REV 2:7](https://ref.ly/Rev2:7), [REV 2:11](https://ref.ly/Rev2:11), [REV 2:17](https://ref.ly/Rev2:17), [REV 2:26–2:28](https://ref.ly/Rev2:26-Rev2:28), [REV 3:5](https://ref.ly/Rev3:5), [REV 3:12](https://ref.ly/Rev3:12), [REV 3:21](https://ref.ly/Rev3:21)

### The heavenly treasure is to be sought

**[MAT 6:19–6:21](https://ref.ly/Matt6:19-Matt6:21)** *See also* [MAT 13:44](https://ref.ly/Matt13:44), [MAT 19:21](https://ref.ly/Matt19:21); [LUK 12:33](https://ref.ly/Luke12:33); [2CO 4:18](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:18); [PHP 3:8](https://ref.ly/Phil3:8); [1TI 6:18–6:19](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:18-1Tim6:19); [REV 3:18](https://ref.ly/Rev3:18)

Heavenly rewards
----------------

### Service will be rewarded in heaven

**[1CO 3:11–3:14](https://ref.ly/1Cor3:11-1Cor3:14)** *See also* [MAT 5:12](https://ref.ly/Matt5:12) parallel [LUK 6:23](https://ref.ly/Luke6:23); [REV 22:12](https://ref.ly/Rev22:12)

### The prospect of heavenly rewards should be a spur to present service

**[PHP 3:14](https://ref.ly/Phil3:14)** *See also* [HEB 11:26](https://ref.ly/Heb11:26)

### Rewards will vary

**[MAT 16:27](https://ref.ly/Matt16:27)** *See also* [DAN 12:3](https://ref.ly/Dan12:3); [MAT 25:20–25:23](https://ref.ly/Matt25:20-Matt25:23) parallel [LUK 19:15–19:19](https://ref.ly/Luke19:15-Luke19:19); [1CO 3:8](https://ref.ly/1Cor3:8); [2CO 9:6](https://ref.ly/2Cor9:6); [REV 22:12](https://ref.ly/Rev22:12)

### Endurance for Jesus Christ's sake will be specially rewarded

**[MAT 5:10–5:12](https://ref.ly/Matt5:10-Matt5:12)** parallel [LUK 6:22–6:23](https://ref.ly/Luke6:22-Luke6:23)

### Rewards for service include crowns signifying position and authority

**[1PE 5:4](https://ref.ly/1Pet5:4)** *See also* [1TH 2:19](https://ref.ly/1Thess2:19); [2TI 4:8](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:8)

### The redeemed will share Jesus Christ's position in glory

**[EPH 2:6](https://ref.ly/Eph2:6)** *See also* [JHN 14:3](https://ref.ly/John14:3), [JHN 17:24](https://ref.ly/John17:24); [1JN 3:2](https://ref.ly/1John3:2); [REV 22:4](https://ref.ly/Rev22:4)

The resurrection body as a heavenly inheritance
-----------------------------------------------

**[PHP 3:20–3:21](https://ref.ly/Phil3:20-Phil3:21)** *See also* [1CO 15:42–15:44](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:42-1Cor15:44); [2CO 5:1–5:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:1-2Cor5:4)

## 9414: heaven, as community of the redeemed (id: 9414)

The community of the redeemed in heaven will represent all peoples and languages. They will owe this solely to the sacrifice of Jesus Christ. They will share in the divine life in perfect fellowship with God, free for ever from suffering and death.

Heaven as a divine gift
-----------------------

**[ROM 6:23](https://ref.ly/Rom6:23)** *See also* [LUK 12:32](https://ref.ly/Luke12:32), [LUK 22:28–22:30](https://ref.ly/Luke22:28-Luke22:30); [JHN 17:2](https://ref.ly/John17:2)

Divine preparations made for believers in heaven
------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 14:2](https://ref.ly/John14:2)** *See also* [2CO 5:1](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:1); [HEB 11:16](https://ref.ly/Heb11:16)

The redeemed in heaven come from all peoples
--------------------------------------------

**[REV 7:9–7:10](https://ref.ly/Rev7:9-Rev7:10)** *See also* [ISA 59:19](https://ref.ly/Isa59:19); [MAL 1:11](https://ref.ly/Mal1:11); [MAT 8:11](https://ref.ly/Matt8:11) parallel [LUK 13:29](https://ref.ly/Luke13:29); [REV 5:9](https://ref.ly/Rev5:9)

The redeemed owe their place in heaven solely to Jesus Christ
-------------------------------------------------------------

**[REV 7:14](https://ref.ly/Rev7:14)** *Washing one's robes in the blood of the Lamb symbolises cleansing through the sacrifice of Jesus Christ.* *See also* [1PE 1:18–1:19](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:18-1Pet1:19); [REV 22:14](https://ref.ly/Rev22:14)

The redeemed are identified with Jesus Christ
---------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ acknowledges the redeemed as his own

**[LUK 12:8](https://ref.ly/Luke12:8)** *See also* [MAT 7:21–7:23](https://ref.ly/Matt7:21-Matt7:23)

### Believers possess the family likeness to Jesus Christ

**[1CO 15:49](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:49)** *See also* [2CO 3:18](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:18); [PHP 3:21](https://ref.ly/Phil3:21); [1JN 3:2](https://ref.ly/1John3:2)

### Believers share divine life

**[2PE 1:4](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:4)** *See also* [REV 2:7](https://ref.ly/Rev2:7), [REV 3:21](https://ref.ly/Rev3:21)

Believers on earth at the second coming will be taken up to heaven
------------------------------------------------------------------

**[REV 11:12](https://ref.ly/Rev11:12)** *See also* [JHN 11:26](https://ref.ly/John11:26); [1TH 4:16–4:17](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:16-1Thess4:17) *Believers living on earth when Jesus Christ returns will not experience death, but be taken straight to heaven.*

Conditions in heaven for the redeemed
-------------------------------------

### Perpetual and perfect fellowship with the Lord

**[REV 21:3](https://ref.ly/Rev21:3)** *See also* [PSA 17:15](https://ref.ly/Ps17:15); [MAT 5:8](https://ref.ly/Matt5:8); [JHN 14:3](https://ref.ly/John14:3); [1TH 4:17](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:17); [REV 22:4](https://ref.ly/Rev22:4)

### Joy in the immediate presence of God

**[PSA 16:11](https://ref.ly/Ps16:11)** *See also* [ISA 51:11](https://ref.ly/Isa51:11); [MAT 25:21](https://ref.ly/Matt25:21); [LUK 15:7](https://ref.ly/Luke15:7), [LUK 15:10](https://ref.ly/Luke15:10); [JHN 15:11](https://ref.ly/John15:11); [1TH 2:19–2:20](https://ref.ly/1Thess2:19-1Thess2:20); [HEB 12:2](https://ref.ly/Heb12:2), [HEB 12:22](https://ref.ly/Heb12:22); [JUD 1:24](https://ref.ly/Jude1:24)

### Restfulness

## 9420: book of life (id: 9420)

Book in which the names of the living were recorded and from which their names were removed at death. From the time of the exodus onwards, Scripture contains references to God's book of life. It is to contain only the names of the righteous and is to be opened on the day of judgment.

The privilege of having one's name in the book of life
------------------------------------------------------

**[LUK 10:20](https://ref.ly/Luke10:20)**; **[HEB 12:22–12:23](https://ref.ly/Heb12:22-Heb12:23)** *See also* [DAN 12:1](https://ref.ly/Dan12:1); [PHP 4:3](https://ref.ly/Phil4:3); [REV 3:5](https://ref.ly/Rev3:5), [REV 21:27](https://ref.ly/Rev21:27)

The unrighteous are excluded from the book of life
--------------------------------------------------

**[EXO 32:31–32:33](https://ref.ly/Exod32:31-Exod32:33)** *See also* [PSA 69:27–69:28](https://ref.ly/Ps69:27-Ps69:28); [REV 13:8](https://ref.ly/Rev13:8), [REV 17:8](https://ref.ly/Rev17:8), [REV 20:12–20:15](https://ref.ly/Rev20:12-Rev20:15)

Other references to such a book
-------------------------------

[PSA 56:8](https://ref.ly/Ps56:8), [PSA 139:16](https://ref.ly/Ps139:16); ; [MAL 3:16](https://ref.ly/Mal3:16)

* **Associated Passages:** Luke 10:20; Hebrews 12:22-23; Daniel 12:1; Philippians 4:3; Revelation 3:5; Revelation 21:27; Exodus 32:31-33; Psalms 69:27-28; Revelation 13:8; Revelation 17:8; Revelation 20:12-15; Psalms 56:8; Psalms 139:16; Malachi 3:16
* **Associated Articles:** 5232: book (ID: `5232@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9210: judgment, God's (ID: `9210@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9230: judgment seat (ID: `9230@DictionaryBibleThemes`)

* **Associated Articles:** 9510: hell (ID: `9510@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9520: Abyss, the (ID: `9520@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9530: Hades (ID: `9530@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9540: Sheol (ID: `9540@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 9510: hell (id: 9510)

A term used in English translations of the Bible to represent the Hebrew word “Sheol” (the place of the departed) and the Greek word “Gehenna”, which came to refer to the place of punishment for the wicked after death. The Valley of Hinnom (Hebrew “Ge Hinnom”, from which “Gehenna” is derived) on the south side of Jerusalem became a symbol of all that is hateful to God, on account of its use for human sacrifice.

* **Associated Articles:** 9511: hell, as a place of punishment (ID: `9511@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9512: hell, as an experience (ID: `9512@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9513: hell, as incentive to action (ID: `9513@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 9511: hell, as a place of punishment (id: 9511)

The place of eternal punishment in fire and darkness intended for Satan and his angels, but also for human beings who choose to reject God.

Hell was originally created for the devil and his angels
--------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 25:41](https://ref.ly/Matt25:41)** *See also* [LUK 8:31](https://ref.ly/Luke8:31); [2PE 2:4](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:4); [REV 20:1–20:3](https://ref.ly/Rev20:1-Rev20:3), [REV 20:10](https://ref.ly/Rev20:10)

Hell is a consequence of rejecting God
--------------------------------------

**[MAT 13:40–13:42](https://ref.ly/Matt13:40-Matt13:42)** *See also* [DEU 32:22](https://ref.ly/Deut32:22) *Fire is often referred to in the OT as a symbol of divine judgment*; [MRK 9:42–9:48](https://ref.ly/Mark9:42-Mark9:48); [JHN 3:36](https://ref.ly/John3:36); [ROM 2:8](https://ref.ly/Rom2:8); [1TH 5:9](https://ref.ly/1Thess5:9); [HEB 10:26–10:29](https://ref.ly/Heb10:26-Heb10:29); [2PE 3:7](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:7); [REV 20:15](https://ref.ly/Rev20:15), [REV 21:8](https://ref.ly/Rev21:8)

Jesus Christ possesses authority over hell
------------------------------------------

**[MAT 16:18](https://ref.ly/Matt16:18)**; **[REV 1:18](https://ref.ly/Rev1:18)** *The Greek word “Hades” often simply means “death”. However, at points it implies the experience of punishment after death.* *See also* [JHN 5:27](https://ref.ly/John5:27); [ACT 10:42](https://ref.ly/Acts10:42), [ACT 17:31](https://ref.ly/Acts17:31)

## 9512: hell, as an experience (id: 9512)

The state of final separation from God, and so from all light, love, peace, pleasure and fulfilment.

Hell is separation from God
---------------------------

**[2TH 1:8–1:10](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:8-2Thess1:10)** *See also* [MAT 7:23](https://ref.ly/Matt7:23), [MAT 8:12](https://ref.ly/Matt8:12), [MAT 25:32](https://ref.ly/Matt25:32); [REV 21:8](https://ref.ly/Rev21:8)

The final state of the wicked is one of eternal punishment
----------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 25:41–25:46](https://ref.ly/Matt25:41-Matt25:46)** *“eternal punishment” means the punishment that is part of, and belongs to, the final order of things that follows this present age. This is usually, though not invariably, understood as an unending process of punishment consciously experienced by the wicked.* *See also* [JUD 1:7](https://ref.ly/Jude1:7)

## 9520: Abyss, the (id: 9520)

Derived from a Greek word meaning “something which is bottomless” and often used to refer to a place of despair in which demons are imprisoned.

The Abyss as a place of despair
-------------------------------

[LUK 8:31](https://ref.ly/Luke8:31); ; [REV 9:2](https://ref.ly/Rev9:2)

The Abyss as the home of demons
-------------------------------

[REV 9:11](https://ref.ly/Rev9:11), [REV 17:8](https://ref.ly/Rev17:8)

The Abyss as a prison
---------------------

## 9530: Hades (id: 9530)

A term used in the NT to refer to the place in which departed spirits rest, while waiting for judgment.

Hades is the place where the dead wait for judgment
---------------------------------------------------

**[REV 20:13–20:14](https://ref.ly/Rev20:13-Rev20:14)** *See also* [MAT 11:23](https://ref.ly/Matt11:23) parallel [LUK 10:15](https://ref.ly/Luke10:15) *translated “depths”*; [LUK 16:23](https://ref.ly/Luke16:23) *translated “hell”*[ACT 2:27](https://ref.ly/Acts2:27), [ACT 2:31](https://ref.ly/Acts2:31)[REV 6:8](https://ref.ly/Rev6:8)

-----------------------------

**[MAT 16:18](https://ref.ly/Matt16:18)**; **[REV 1:18](https://ref.ly/Rev1:18)**

## 9540: Sheol (id: 9540)

A Hebrew term used to refer to the grave, the pit or the tomb. Some older translations have the term incorrectly translated as “hell”.

Sheol is the destiny of all
---------------------------

**[PSA 89:48](https://ref.ly/Ps89:48)** *See also* [GEN 37:35](https://ref.ly/Gen37:35), [GEN 44:29](https://ref.ly/Gen44:29); [1KI 2:9](https://ref.ly/1Kgs2:9); [PSA 18:5](https://ref.ly/Ps18:5), [PSA 107:20](https://ref.ly/Ps107:20); [PRO 1:12](https://ref.ly/Prov1:12), [PRO 30:16](https://ref.ly/Prov30:16); [EZK 31:15–31:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek31:15-Ezek31:17); [JON 2:2](https://ref.ly/Jonah2:2)

Sheol is often described in terms suggesting a grave
----------------------------------------------------

**[PSA 88:11–88:12](https://ref.ly/Ps88:11-Ps88:12)** *See also* [JOB 3:13–3:19](https://ref.ly/Job3:13-Job3:19), [JOB 7:9](https://ref.ly/Job7:9), [JOB 17:13–17:16](https://ref.ly/Job17:13-Job17:16); [PSA 6:5](https://ref.ly/Ps6:5); [ECC 9:10](https://ref.ly/Eccl9:10); [ISA 14:9–14:11](https://ref.ly/Isa14:9-Isa14:11), [ISA 38:18](https://ref.ly/Isa38:18)

To go to Sheol was regarded as a punishment
-------------------------------------------

---------------------------

## 9600: Hope (id: 9600)

* 9610: hope
* **Associated Articles:** 9610: hope (ID: `9610@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 9610: hope (id: 9610)

In Scripture, a confident expectation for the future, describing both the act of hoping and the object hoped for. When grounded in God, hope provides the motivation to live the Christian life even in the face of trouble.

* **Associated Articles:** 9611: hope, nature of (ID: `9611@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9612: hope, in God (ID: `9612@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9613: hope, as confidence (ID: `9613@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9614: hope, results of its absence (ID: `9614@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9615: hope, results of (ID: `9615@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 9611: hope, nature of (id: 9611)

Hope, in its general sense, is the anticipation of a future outcome. It is a subjective expectation which may be either firmly based or misdirected.

Hope that an event will take place
----------------------------------

**[1CO 9:10](https://ref.ly/1Cor9:10)**; **[1TI 3:14](https://ref.ly/1Tim3:14)** *See also* [EST 9:1](https://ref.ly/Esth9:1); [LUK 6:34](https://ref.ly/Luke6:34); [ACT 24:26](https://ref.ly/Acts24:26) *Felix hoped Paul would offer him a bribe*; [ROM 15:24](https://ref.ly/Rom15:24) *Paul hoped to visit Rome on his way to Spain*; [1CO 9:15](https://ref.ly/1Cor9:15), [1CO 16:7](https://ref.ly/1Cor16:7); [2CO 1:13–1:14](https://ref.ly/2Cor1:13-2Cor1:14), [2CO 5:11](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:11), [2CO 11:1](https://ref.ly/2Cor11:1)PHP [2:19](https://ref.ly/2Cor2:19), [PHP 2:23](https://ref.ly/Phil2:23)[PHM 1:22](https://ref.ly/Phlm1:22); [2JN 1:12](https://ref.ly/2John1:12); [3JN 1:14](https://ref.ly/3John1:14)

Hope for a positive outcome
---------------------------

**[ECC 9:4](https://ref.ly/Eccl9:4)** *See also* [RUT 1:12](https://ref.ly/Ruth1:12); [2KI 4:28](https://ref.ly/2Kgs4:28); [PRO 19:18](https://ref.ly/Prov19:18); [ROM 11:14](https://ref.ly/Rom11:14)

----------------------

**[PSA 33:17](https://ref.ly/Ps33:17)**; **[JER 23:16](https://ref.ly/Jer23:16)** *See also* [JOB 8:13–8:14](https://ref.ly/Job8:13-Job8:14), [JOB 11:20](https://ref.ly/Job11:20); [PRO 26:12](https://ref.ly/Prov26:12), [PRO 29:20](https://ref.ly/Prov29:20); [JER 50:7](https://ref.ly/Jer50:7); [1TI 6:17](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:17)

-----------------------------

**[JOB 30:26](https://ref.ly/Job30:26)**; **[JER 8:15](https://ref.ly/Jer8:15)** *See also* [JOB 6:19–6:20](https://ref.ly/Job6:19-Job6:20), [JOB 14:7–14:12](https://ref.ly/Job14:7-Job14:12), [JOB 19:10](https://ref.ly/Job19:10), [JOB 27:8](https://ref.ly/Job27:8); [ISA 38:18](https://ref.ly/Isa38:18); [JER 13:16](https://ref.ly/Jer13:16), [JER 14:19](https://ref.ly/Jer14:19); [LAM 3:18](https://ref.ly/Lam3:18); [EZK 37:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:11); [ZEC 9:5](https://ref.ly/Zech9:5); [LUK 24:21](https://ref.ly/Luke24:21) *The two disciples share their hopes with Jesus Christ on the Emmaus road*; [1TH 4:13](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:13)

## 9612: hope, in God (id: 9612)

A total grounding of one's confidence and expectation in God's goodness and providential care even in the face of trouble.

Hope in God is commanded
------------------------

**[PSA 131:3](https://ref.ly/Ps131:3)**; **[1TI 6:17](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:17)** *See also* [PSA 31:24](https://ref.ly/Ps31:24), [PSA 130:7](https://ref.ly/Ps130:7); [ROM 12:12](https://ref.ly/Rom12:12); [HEB 10:23](https://ref.ly/Heb10:23)

--------------------------------------------------

## 9613: hope, as confidence (id: 9613)

Hope means more than a vague wish that something will happen. It is a sure and confident expectation in God's future faithfulness and presence. The horizon of Christian hope extends beyond death into an eternity prepared by God himself, the reality of which is guaranteed by Jesus Christ.

God and Jesus Christ are the hope of believers
----------------------------------------------

**[PSA 71:5](https://ref.ly/Ps71:5)**; **[1TI 1:1](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:1)** *See also* [JER 14:8](https://ref.ly/Jer14:8), [JER 17:13](https://ref.ly/Jer17:13); [MAT 12:21](https://ref.ly/Matt12:21); [ISA 42:4](https://ref.ly/Isa42:4); [ACT 28:20](https://ref.ly/Acts28:20); [ROM 15:12–15:13](https://ref.ly/Rom15:12-Rom15:13); [ISA 11:10](https://ref.ly/Isa11:10); [1TI 4:10](https://ref.ly/1Tim4:10); [1PE 1:21](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:21)

The hope of resurrection and eternal life
-----------------------------------------

## 9614: hope, results of its absence (id: 9614)

An absence of hope leads to a loss of vision, a sense of despondency and ultimately to despair. This contrasts sharply with the Christian hope.

Feelings produced by a lack of hope
-----------------------------------

### Despair

**[JOB 17:13–17:15](https://ref.ly/Job17:13-Job17:15)**; **[PRO 13:12](https://ref.ly/Prov13:12)**; **[1CH 29:15](https://ref.ly/1Chr29:15)** *See also* [JOB 6:11](https://ref.ly/Job6:11), [JOB 7:6](https://ref.ly/Job7:6); [PSA 88:15–88:18](https://ref.ly/Ps88:15-Ps88:18); [ECC 2:17](https://ref.ly/Eccl2:17); [ISA 19:9](https://ref.ly/Isa19:9), [ISA 38:18](https://ref.ly/Isa38:18); [2CO 1:8](https://ref.ly/2Cor1:8)

### A sense of being abandoned by God

**[PSA 22:1–22:2](https://ref.ly/Ps22:1-Ps22:2)** *See also* [LAM 3:18](https://ref.ly/Lam3:18); [EZK 37:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:11)

### A deep longing for life to end

**[1KI 19:4](https://ref.ly/1Kgs19:4)**; **[JOB 3:20–3:21](https://ref.ly/Job3:20-Job3:21)**; **[ECC 4:1–4:2](https://ref.ly/Eccl4:1-Eccl4:2)** *See also* [GEN 27:46](https://ref.ly/Gen27:46); [NUM 11:15](https://ref.ly/Num11:15); [JOB 7:13–7:15](https://ref.ly/Job7:13-Job7:15); [JER 8:3](https://ref.ly/Jer8:3); [JON 4:3](https://ref.ly/Jonah4:3), [JON 4:8](https://ref.ly/Jonah4:8); [REV 9:6](https://ref.ly/Rev9:6)

-----------------------------

### The choice of trusting in God or futile self\-effort

**[ROM 4:18](https://ref.ly/Rom4:18)** *See also* [JON 1:13–1:14](https://ref.ly/Jonah1:13-Jonah1:14); [JER 18:11–18:12](https://ref.ly/Jer18:11-Jer18:12); [ACT 27:20](https://ref.ly/Acts27:20)

## 9615: hope, results of (id: 9615)

Hope gives believers confidence and reassurance in this present life, allowing them to lead effective lives for God. It also reassures them of the reality of eternal life, allowing them to face death with confidence.

Hope reassures believers in this present life
---------------------------------------------

### Hope reassures believers in their faith

**[HEB 3:6](https://ref.ly/Heb3:6)** *See also* [EPH 1:18–1:19](https://ref.ly/Eph1:18-Eph1:19); [HEB 7:18–7:22](https://ref.ly/Heb7:18-Heb7:22), [HEB 10:23](https://ref.ly/Heb10:23)

### Hope encourages believers

**[PSA 31:2](https://ref.ly/Ps31:2)** *See also* [ISA 40:31](https://ref.ly/Isa40:31), [ISA 49:23](https://ref.ly/Isa49:23); [ROM 5:3–5:5](https://ref.ly/Rom5:3-Rom5:5)

### Hope encourages believers to rejoice

**[ROM 12:12](https://ref.ly/Rom12:12)** *See also* [ROM 5:1–5:2](https://ref.ly/Rom5:1-Rom5:2)

### Hope encourages believers to look for restoration

[PSA 37:9](https://ref.ly/Ps37:9); ; [JER 14:8](https://ref.ly/Jer14:8), [JER 31:17](https://ref.ly/Jer31:17); ; [LAM 3:29–3:31](https://ref.ly/Lam3:29-Lam3:31); ; [HOS 2:15](https://ref.ly/Hos2:15); ; [ZEC 9:12](https://ref.ly/Zech9:12)
